Current Commentary

Reflections on the Constitutional Debate 58

Since the Legislative Yuan established the Constitution Drafting Committee, the drafter has been burying his head in drafting the initial draft amidst the serious national crisis, and it has recently appeared in newspapers. Subsequently, various reviews have emerged, with mixed praise and criticism and much discussion. The country's situation is as precarious as a pile of eggs, yet scholars are able to concentrate on this alone, engaging in endless debates. Could it be that they also feel the sentiment of "saving the country through the constitution"? In this regard, this newspaper dares not make any claims. Those who criticize us may be like those who blame summer insects for not being able to speak of ice.

Drafting a constitution is a major policy of the country. France issued constitutions ten times from 1789 to 1875. From the beginning of the revolution to the Directorate period, constitution expert Sieyès participated in the process. His desk was full of draft constitutions. However, is reading the Classic of Filial Piety enough to repel thieves? Can simply drafting a constitution avoid the political turmoil and terror in France at that time? Precedents in constitutional history are clearly traceable. Therefore, it is difficult to guarantee whether borrowing a constitution to save the country from danger will succeed. However, current discussions focus solely on the strengths and weaknesses of constitution drafting techniques, while neglecting the prior issues that are a hundred times more important than constitution drafting techniques. Abandoning the important for the trivial and rushing the slow cannot but cause doubt.

In the current discussions on the draft constitution, some criticize the government for "not specially hiring experts in a solemn manner to establish a committee to draft it, but instead entrusting it to the Legislative Yuan, a government agency composed of officials." Others criticize it for "being compiled according to the Three Principles of the People, resulting in extremely clumsy chapter arrangements in terms of legislative technique." Still others criticize it for not calling the "Republic of China a Republic based on the Three Principles of the People." The questions raised are indeed reasonable. However, it is also very easy to act as a defense attorney for the draft. In the past, Napoleon ordered Baudry, Tronchet, Pigeau, and Maleville to draft the Civil Code. He pointed to the four and said, "I give you six months to create a Civil Code for me." The four humbly retreated and competed to cooperate under Napoleon's whip. The Civil Code was eventually completed and has been promulgated for a hundred years. Considering the past, Napoleon never had a solemn ceremony. The key to drafting laws lies not in the solemnity of the form, but in the effectiveness of the substance. This can be used as the first defense for the initial draft. The chapters of the constitution are not immutable. Legislative technique is not a rigid and inflexible path. The French Constitution of 1875 is fragmented and unsystematic, let alone chapter arrangements. The German Weimar Constitution is extremely detailed and differs greatly from various past constitutions. The Soviet Constitution is even more innovative. Classical constitutional scholars consider it shocking. Therefore, compiling it according to the Three Principles of the People is not surprising. Moreover, the purpose-based compilation method is superior to the form-based compilation method. This can be used as the second defense for the initial draft. As for calling the Republic of China a Republic based on the Three Principles of the People, it is not an innovation. The Soviet Union calls itself the "Soviet Socialist Russian Federal Republic," which is clear evidence. This can be used as the third defense for the initial draft. As for the remaining points of contention, each has its own perspective. The drafter may have omissions, but onlookers are clear-minded and can point out the flaws. The more reason is debated, the clearer it becomes. It is the responsibility of scholars to evaluate the strengths and weaknesses, so there is no need to be emotional. However, we cannot remain silent if those who debate the constitution focus on the strengths and weaknesses of constitution drafting techniques while ignoring the prior issues that are a hundred times more important than constitution drafting techniques.

What is the prior issue in drafting a constitution? The life of a constitution does not lie in the hands of the lawmakers, but in the hands of those who implement the constitution. If the lawmakers' responsibility is to internally consult the spirit of the nation and externally consider the trends of the world, striving to make the draft constitution a reflection of the nation's most urgent needs, then they have already done their utmost. As for how to use the constitution to implement it without obstruction and to make it effective, how to make the constitution evolve into a living life and not become a dead formality, even the most intelligent and talented lawmakers cannot solve it. The task of lawmakers is limited to technique, while how to promote and maximize benefits depends on those responsible for political operations. In the past, the German scholar Savigny believed that the relationship between law and lawmakers was a "technical element," and the relationship between law and national life was a "political element." He believed that the political element was more important than the technical element. Although his theory is inevitably flawed in terms of obliterating the value of written law, the actual effectiveness of the law must be emphasized, which is the consensus of the general public.

According to the actual effectiveness of the constitution, it not only requires legislative techniques that meet actual needs but also requires a strong interest in constitution drafting. What is a strong interest in constitution drafting? It is the movement to fight for the constitution. The development of constitutionalism in Europe and America is often driven by the self-struggle of the people. The people shed blood and fought, one after another, and only after a long period of resistance did they obtain the power to draft a constitution. Therefore, the people regard the constitution as a treasure, and everyone has a heart to protect the constitution. The government naturally does not dare to destroy the constitution. The German scholar Ihering once said, "A law that has not been obtained through struggle is like a lost child picked up on the street and is not worthy of cherishing. If it is born from oneself and one wants to take it away from the mother's arms, then the mother will definitely roar and refuse to give up." These words are wise. Do those who discuss the constitution today recognize that this constitution in the making is a lost child lost by someone else, or a beloved child in the mother's arms? If this question is not resolved, then all discussions of technical issues are nothing but a waste of words.

Now let us look back at the situation of our country and the situation of the people. The territory is shrinking day by day, the population is decreasing day by day, unemployment is rampant in cities, rural areas are on the verge of bankruptcy, floods and droughts continue unabated, internal warfare and fires are rising one after another, bandits are everywhere, and taxes are heavy. People are struggling to protect their lives, let alone participating in politics or fighting for rights. The authorities are working hard to plan for the country, loudly calling for unification and saving the country from danger through the constitution. However, in reality, the obstacles to unification are only a few warlords and politicians. These people prefer to have no laws. Now, wanting to use a piece of paper to offer to these people in order to promote unification is almost like seeking a tiger for its skin. Our country has created laws that are voluminous, but the country has never received the effect of the rule of law, and the people have never received actual protection. The powerful always regard the law as a trifle. Clearly there are laws to follow, but they must seek it outside the law. The effectiveness of the law is minimal, and the people naturally have no possibility of abiding by the law. How close is the relationship between law and society? If there is no fundamental connection, then what will be the use of talking about constitution drafting every day? May those who discuss the constitution today pay attention to this prior issue.

The End of the British-Russian Trade War 59

The British King Signs an Order to Withdraw the Ban on Russian Goods

Effective Immediately After the Release of the Two British Engineers

The Restoration of Diplomatic Relations Between the United States and Russia Removes a Small Obstacle

(London) The British-Russian trade war ended today. The British King signed an order this afternoon to withdraw the ban on the import of Russian goods, effective immediately after Moscow releases the two British engineers. This is the result of the fourth meeting this morning between British Foreign Secretary Simon and Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Commissioner Litvinov. Initially, the Russian side insisted that Britain lift the ban first, and then Russia would release the people. It was not until today's meeting that it was agreed that both parties would implement it simultaneously: the two engineers would be released and deported by Russia immediately. In addition, the Russian side also withdrew various retaliatory plans for business, and the two countries immediately reopened negotiations to conclude a trade agreement. It is rumored that both sides plan to issue a formal exchange of letters detailing the agreed-upon methods, which is expected to be announced on Sunday afternoon. It is now said that after the resolution of the British-Russian trade war, it can also remove a small obstacle to the United States' recognition of Soviet Russia. (A Dispatch from the Guomin Agency on the 1st)

European Gold Bloc Proposes Joint Effort with US to Curb Currency Speculation 60

Economic Conference Extended

Awaiting White House Response

(London) After a day and a night of precarious uncertainty, the fate of the World Economic Conference now hinges on a final plan to curb exchange rate volatility and protect the gold standard, awaiting the US President's response. Newspaper dispatches indicate the proposal is likely satisfactory to the US President and has already been accepted by US Undersecretary of State Moley, pending only presidential approval. Washington sources say the President sees no objection to central banks engaging in efforts to curb exchange rate fluctuations, but believes temporary stabilization is the responsibility of these banks, not the government. Commentators suggest that, based on this news, the President has, in principle, approved the European plan.

This plan was drafted by England, France, Italy, the Netherlands, Belgium, and Switzerland, and discussed with Moley. It reportedly contains the following three points:

(1) The aforementioned countries (including the United States) will issue a joint declaration guaranteeing central bank cooperation to prevent speculative exchange rate fluctuations.

(2) The declaration will solemnly reaffirm the importance of not undermining the stability of the gold standard.

(3) All countries agree to focus on the goals of the World Economic Conference, namely the eventual restoration of the gold standard.

It has now been agreed that once formal US presidential approval is received, British Prime Minister MacDonald will invite the chief representatives to 10 Downing Street to sign the declaration. The wording of the declaration will reportedly allow the United States to freely implement its monetary policy, with central banks merely declaring war on speculators.

In the event that the United States is unwilling to join the joint declaration, it is reported that the gold standard countries will form a strong gold bloc and, under any agreement, the gold standard will maintain its position through a joint declaration.

The situation today is extremely tense, and even Chairman MacDonald is deeply concerned about the conference's breakdown. It is said that MacDonald is considering inviting all European foreign ministers to London next week to join an expanded conference to intensify the work. (National Telegram, 30th)

(London) It is reported that the declaration discussed by the gold bloc also contains a general expression of hope that central banks will take joint action to curb currency speculation. (Reuters, 1st)

(London) Discussions on the issue of currency stabilization have entered a new phase today. Representatives from all countries, including the US, have agreed on common language regarding the gold issue. This proposal has now been sent to President Roosevelt. It is reported that the President is insisting on revisions regarding the stabilization section. The conference has been extended to tomorrow to await the President's response. The main points of the proposal put forward by the gold bloc are as follows: All countries currently on the gold standard must maintain it, and countries that have abandoned the gold standard should restore it when possible. As for the stability ratio and the stability period, each country must decide for itself. Currently, gold standard countries are firmly determined to strive to maintain their position, and countries with depreciated currencies support the position taken by the gold standard countries. The language of the gold proposal is the result of a day-long effort to reconcile differing views. Representatives of the gold bloc discussed for a long time in the afternoon. The final draft was studied by US representative Professor Moley, French Finance Minister Bonnet, Italian Finance Minister Jung, and British government economic advisor Ross. Everyone believes that a declaration in which the United States can participate is more valuable than a purely European declaration. Representatives from various countries held closed-door meetings with their experts to discuss this matter. (Reuters, 30th)

(London) As of 11 a.m. this morning, the President of the United States had not yet responded to the latest proposal to curb exchange rate speculation. It is reported that the gold standard countries are prepared to continue discussions tentatively at the end of this week and are unlikely to meet again before Monday. (National Telegram, 1st)

(New York) The New York Times correspondent summarized President Roosevelt's views as follows: (1) The dollar has not rotated. (2) The dollar has not fallen to a level where its price can be appropriately stabilized. (3) The position of the United States in the World Economic Conference will be harmed by fixing the dollar price at this time. (Reuters, 1st)

(London) The world is eagerly awaiting President Roosevelt's judgment on the currency plan, knowing that the future of the Economic Conference and the prospects for European stability depend on it. The proposed declaration is not related to currency stabilization but aims to curb speculation. The gold bloc initially demanded immediate stabilization of currency prices, which the US and Britain opposed. The gold bloc has now agreed to change its attitude because of the proposal for international unanimity in rejecting speculation. It seems that President Roosevelt may be willing to have the Federal Reserve Bank work to curb speculation in the foreign exchange market, so as to avoid violent fluctuations in the dollar exchange rate. Professor Moley has already approved the compromise plan now submitted to the President, so the President should approve today the proposal that the central banks of various countries should use their power to curb speculation. If the United States accepts this declaration, the governments of various countries will eventually decide the timing of currency stabilization, or at present, but this period is of course not yet negotiable. The US delegation did not participate in yesterday's negotiations, indicating that the US representatives believe that the attitude of the United States on this issue is not within the purview of the US delegation. (Reuters, 1st)

(London) The plan to resolve the currency crisis was telegraphed to President Roosevelt yesterday. Representatives from various countries at the World Economic Conference are now awaiting his response. It is expected that the reply will arrive tonight, at which time British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon may convene a meeting of the gold bloc and other related countries to consider the reply. The content of the reply has aroused general speculation. The US delegation in London believes that the President will revise the plan and not focus too much on gold. The President will express his sympathy for the gold bloc but will not express concrete views on the gold standard. The foreign exchange market was not affected by the expectation of a satisfactory reply. Transactions proceeded as usual on Saturday morning and closed very late. Dollar trading was suddenly active, with many sales. The market closed half an hour later than usual. The dollar exchange rate opened at $4.275, then weakened and fell to $4.33. Near the close, the price recovered slightly to $4.3175. All gold coins were extremely stable. According to Reuters Paris, regardless of the President's reply, the French government clearly expressed its position at this morning's cabinet meeting. After considering Finance Minister Bonnet's report, the Cabinet reiterated its position that nothing can be achieved in the economic scope of the Economic Conference without currency stability. There was no meeting of the conference today, so the Geological Museum was sparsely populated today, but representatives from several countries took the opportunity to explain their positions. The most important was the speech by the Mexican representative, who argued that silver should be a supplementary coin to gold and that silver should not be regarded merely as a commodity, as France has suggested, but that all silver issues should be submitted to the Monetary and Financial Committee for handling. French newspapers have generally sympathetic views towards England, acknowledging that England is in a difficult position on the currency issue. (Reuters, 1st)

Temporary Currency Stabilization is the Responsibility of the Banking Sector 64

President Roosevelt's Statement

Campobello Island When reporters asked President Roosevelt about reports from British officials in London that the President supported an agreement to prevent violent currency fluctuations, the President reportedly replied that temporary stabilization was a matter for the banks, not a government problem, and was not within the scope of the World Economic Conference. Furthermore, the stabilization issue was extremely complex and could not be resolved by the Economic Conference in a few days or weeks. At the same time, he believed that dollar fluctuations would not hinder the US domestic economy. The President expressed doubts about whether gold bloc countries could maintain their position and whether currencies should have permanent stability before they were free to find their true prices. The President believes that, as far as the United States is concerned, the stabilization issue can be temporarily shelved until the Economic Conference achieves other goals, but it is noteworthy that the President did not express opposition to informal cooperation among central banks to reduce fluctuations. Inventor of Movies 80

(National Telegram from Berlin on the 30th) Movies have now become a form of entertainment for people all over the world. There are approximately 100,000 movie theaters in the world. But who would have known that the inventor of movies, after presenting his invention to the world in 1895 and premiering it in Berlin to great acclaim, eventually abandoned his business due to a lack of funds to improve it, allowing others to continue research based on his invention, perfecting it, and profiting immeasurably? Isn't this extremely heartbreaking? Who is this person? It is the German Skladanowsky. He has been living in obscurity in the Pankow district of Berlin for a long time. Italian Air Force Shows Off over the Atlantic 81

Air Minister Leads 24 Expeditionary Aircraft

Crossing Mountains and Oceans to Tour the Chicago World's Fair

One Crashes in the Netherlands, Killing One and Injuring Four

(National Telegram from Austantai on the 1st) As the Italian air force squadron of 24 planes bound for the Chicago World's Fair took off this morning, 3,000 Italians bid them farewell. Air Minister Balbo told reporters before his departure: "I am confident that this trip will be successful. Next time, we will make a round-the-world flight." At dawn this morning, the 24 expeditionary aircraft were lined up on the lake. The instructors of the Naval Academy were busy with final preparations. After the pilots had breakfast at 4:15 a.m., they gathered at the pier. Then Commander Cagna and General Balbo joined them. The military band played the Fascist Party song, the sailors raised the national flag, and after the men saluted, they boarded the gasoline tankers in an orderly fashion amidst cheers from the crowd and said goodbye. Balbo, who was the last to board the ship, shouted, "Long live the country! Long live the king! Long live the prime minister!" At 4:45 a.m., the pilots uncovered the engine covers and took off. Balbo's plane was the first to take off, followed quickly by the others. Within 20 minutes, all 24 planes had left the water, circled several times, and headed for the Alps. In addition to Air Minister General Balbo, Commander Cagna, General Val, and Commander Lang were also in joint command. After receiving the latest weather news, Balbo said that he would fly over the Argentaio Mountains and would be able to reach Amsterdam within six hours. The route would pass through Genoa and Milan, cross the Spruggia Pass in the Alps, and then pass through Zurich and Basel to Amsterdam. The entire route will be divided into six legs: (1) From Austantai to Amsterdam, 750 miles; (2) From Amsterdam across the North Sea to London (Tiley), 525 miles; (3) From London (Tiley) across the Atlantic to Reykjavik, Iceland, 800 miles; (4) From Reykjavik across the Atlantic to Sandwich Bay, Labrador, 1,500 miles; (5) From Sandwich Bay to Montreal, Canada, 1,000 miles; (6) From Montreal to Chicago, 800 miles. The return journey will take the southern route across the Atlantic, passing through New York, the Azores, and Spain. The main purpose of this trip is to show that the Italian air force can make long voyages in a relatively short period of time and with scientific preparation. Beforehand, personnel were sent to the countries that were planned to be passed through to study the weather and aviation situation for nearly two years. After that, meteorological measurements were taken along the way for several months, which shows the thoroughness of the preparation. As for temporary support, four Italian destroyers were dispatched to patrol between Ireland, Iceland, and Greenland, and two submarines and two steam tugs were dispatched to patrol between Iceland and Labrador.

(National Telegram from Amsterdam on the 1st) When the Italian air force squadron arrived here this afternoon, one of the aircraft of the third group, the Red Team's Udine, crashed while landing, killing one and injuring four. The remaining 23 planes landed safely. Air Minister Balbo, who was on the plane, was the first to arrive at 1:02 p.m. Then the planes came one after another. Within three minutes, a total of 16 planes landed safely on the water. The 17th plane was the ill-fated Udine. The last plane arrived at 1:15 p.m. When the Udine landed, the nose suddenly touched the water first. Then the fuselage overturned and the entire plane split apart, with the wooden frame also cracking. One person in the plane drowned after being trapped in the cabin, and the body has not yet been recovered. The remaining four people were injured and were rescued by small boats.

Swiss Women Are the Most Diligent in Housekeeping in the World 82

British Women Do Not Pay Much Attention to Housekeeping

American Women Like Leisure

(Reuters, Prague) A Czech newspaper has compiled a list of the world's most diligent homemakers, but British women are notably absent. It is said that because British women do not pay much attention to housekeeping, it is difficult to calculate the time they spend working each week. Swiss women are the most diligent in housekeeping in the world, working 16 to 17 hours a day. American women like music and only work 68 hours a week, spending about 10 hours a day on housekeeping. The newspaper also said that since the introduction of electricity, coal, and various conveniences into the home, the amount of time modern women spend on housework has been greatly reduced.

Hindenburg Informs Hitler to Maintain Religious Equality 83

Berlin Telegram, 30th of the Month. German President Hindenburg sent a letter to Prime Minister Hitler today, stating that recent efforts by the "German Christians" within the National Socialist Party to impose their will upon the church's doctrines and regulations have caused deep distress among the authorities of the Protestant Church and the general Protestant population, who are witnessing the impact of this political turmoil on the church. Hindenburg further stated that recent disputes between Prussia and church leaders have caused him, as a Christian and head of state, to feel extremely uneasy. "The numerous letters and telegrams I have received recently have proven the shock felt by Protestants due to this controversy. If this situation, with its suppression of spiritual freedom, is allowed to persist, the nation and the fatherland will suffer severely, and the integrity of the state will be compromised. Therefore, I am compelled by my conscience to believe that rescuing this crisis is to uphold God's will. Yesterday, I met with you, and fortunately, you deeply understand this crisis. Therefore, I dare to believe that with your far-sighted political vision, you will be able to use mediation to enable the conflicting representatives within the church and the relevant state organs to work towards the restoration of peace within the church and the integrity of the state."

According to public announcements, after receiving this letter, Hitler immediately ordered Interior Minister Dr. Frick to follow President Hindenburg's wishes and begin mediation efforts. What the future holds for the Catholic Center Party, which the National Socialist Party considers the only obstacle to "German unity," remains undecided. Deliberations among the party's leaders and consultations between its representatives and government authorities are still ongoing today. However, according to those familiar with the details, the current negotiations are no longer about the party's existence but about how its members can join the National Socialist Party. The party's continued existence is considered an irreversible fact.

Beautiful Woman Buys It for £14,500

London Telegram from Havas, 30th of the Month. The original edition of Shakespeare's musical works, formerly owned by the late Lord Rosebery, was auctioned publicly here today and purchased by an American for £14,500.

Austria Opposes Hitler 85

Vienna Telegram, 30th of the Month. Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss declared today that he intends to use the same methods employed by Prime Minister Hitler in Germany to suppress opposition parties to suppress the National Socialist Party in Austria. These strict new regulations will affect all industries and businesses nationwide. From now on, any industry or business must obtain a license. If anyone directly or indirectly promotes National Socialism or Communism in writing or in action, their license will be revoked. To rigorously enforce this ban, Dollfuss has organized an emergency team throughout the country. These team members are loyal and reliable in any emergency. Before joining the team, their daily beliefs must be investigated. Upon joining, they must take an oath to respond within one minute if summoned by the government. Dollfuss has submitted this plan to the cabinet, which immediately passed it, authorizing Dollfuss to issue orders for its implementation. Furthermore, complete control of newspapers is also part of Dollfuss's overall plan. From now on, newspapers will be forced to publish all government announcements and statements so that the people can always be informed of government actions.

Regulations for Flood Prevention Funds in Anhui Province Determined 86

Embankment of Crab Shoal in Fanchang County Collapses

Wuhu Communication. The river tide in Wuhu has not risen or fallen much in recent days, remaining at 27 feet 6 inches. However, due to rain and mountain floods in the inland rivers, the water level in the streets has been rising by one or two inches each day. As a result, the dikes and embankments in the surrounding villages are in imminent danger. Several alarms are reported to the county government every day, and the county government has telegraphed various dike construction associations to strengthen their defenses to prevent collapses. However, the embankment of Crab Shoal in Fanchang County, Anhui Province, suddenly reported an emergency on the 28th, with a breach of over a hundred and several tens of feet long. The embankment is located on the Yangtze River, about thirty miles from Wuhu. The fields within the embankment are extensive. At that time, the situation was extremely serious. County Magistrate Wang Huai of the county went to rescue it in person and rushed to Wuhu to report to the Jiangxi Engineering Bureau and the Second District Administrative Commissioner's Office, requesting assistance. Lin Youlong, the director of the Engineering Bureau, dispatched engineers Ke Tingzhong and Feng Bingxiang to purchase a large amount of reed mats and tree trunks, which were towed by special ships to rescue it, together with the Fanchang fellow villagers in Wuhu. Liu Yiyan, the director of the Anhui Construction Department, had gone to Hangzhou to participate in the opening of the three-province highway and rushed back yesterday. It is said that the flood prevention funds for Anhui Province have been set at 50,000 yuan, and a request for a subsidy of 200,000 yuan from the central government has been approved. Liu returned to the province yesterday afternoon (June 29).

Procedures for Taking Over War Zones 87

Prerequisites After the Establishment of the Takeover Committee

The Most Important Things are the Withdrawal of Japanese Troops and the Disposal of Puppet Troops

Ping Telegram. Although there is still no concrete and definite solution to the Rehe problem, the Japanese withdrawal is only a matter of time. The discussion of reorganization with Li Jichun and others must also have its feasible plan. Taking over the war zone is now the top priority and must be carried out by our side. Therefore, an organization of the takeover committee has been established here and is scheduled to be established on July 1.

The war zone belongs to Hebei Province. Therefore, all arrangements and expenses for the takeover should be borne by the Hebei Provincial Government. The takeover committee has a total of nine members, with Yu Xuezhong as the chairman. As the chairman of Hebei, he should have the responsibility of command. Secondly, Wei Jian, the director of the Hebei Civil Affairs Department, is appointed as the county magistrate and is in charge by Wei. The above two belong to the provincial government. In addition, there are four people belonging to the Political Affairs Committee: Xue Zhiheng, Li Zeyi, Yin Tong, and Liu Shisun. There are two people belonging to the military branch: Tao Shangming and Lei Shourong. There is one person belonging to the transportation aspect: Qian Zongze. If the most suitable distribution of duties is the reorganization, then Yu Xuezhong, Xue Zhiheng, Yin Tong, Lei Shourong, and Liu Shisun bear more responsibility. Secondly, the takeover belongs to Wei Jian, transportation belongs to Qian Zongze and Liu Shisun, guiding the county magistrate belongs to Tao Shangming and Yin Tong, and all contacts belong to Li Zeyi. Each does his best and is suitable for his strengths. The meeting place is set in Tianjin, and the meeting period is until the end of the takeover. The work of the takeover committee is roughly like this.

As for the brief history of the nine members, Yu is the chairman, Wei is the director of the Civil Affairs Department, and Xue Zhiheng is a veteran of the Beiping police circle. He can be very helpful in the reorganization. Li Zeyi is the secretary of the Political Affairs Committee, Yin Tong is a graduate of the military academy, and He Huang are known to be close friends. Liu Shisun is also a graduate of studying in Japan and is also a member of the Political Affairs Committee. Tao Shangming has been working in the Northeast for a long time and was the former foreign affairs section chief of the Northeast. Lei Shourong is also a graduate of the military academy and a staff officer of the General Staff Headquarters. This time, he works in the military branch. Qian Zongze is the vice minister of the Ministry of Railways and the director of the Beining Longhai Railway. Among them, Yin and Liu have been out of officialdom for a long time. This conscription shows their enthusiasm even more.

Once the takeover committee is established, it should proceed with the takeover. There are two prerequisites for the takeover: (1) the withdrawal of Japanese troops; (2) the solution of Li Jichun's troops. If these two things are ready, then the county magistrates will lead the police to take office. After that, everything is just an administrative problem. Therefore, this meeting is called a takeover, but in fact, the more important task is to solve these prerequisites. Regarding the withdrawal of Japanese troops, the original agreement did not limit the date, so it has been delayed. However, at present, the front line has begun to withdraw. However, in military terms, one side withdraws and the other side takes over. There is a need for mutual connection and response. Therefore, those who are prepared to take over must first know the procedures and locations of those who withdraw. Since the Japanese troops began to withdraw, our side has not deeply understood their withdrawal plan. Therefore, it is also very inconvenient to take over. If Japan and I were in combat, we would do our best and drive straight into Ping and have more than enough. However, it is precisely because there must be reasons why they did not enter Ping and could not sustain the war that they reined in on the precipice. Today, the agreement has been reached. Whether it is a gain or loss, let's put it aside. However, since there is an agreement, why not make the withdrawal and takeover seamlessly connected to avoid sudden incidents during the transfer? However, after the agreement was reached, for a month now, the steps of the other party's withdrawal have not been carefully studied, so there is no way to suspend the plan for our takeover. The takeover committee now wants to take over. This is the first thing to start with.

As for Li Jichun's troops, negotiations have been held until now. Whether to reorganize or dismiss them, as long as it is beneficial to the matter, there is no fixed and unchangeable plan. In terms of the number of people, it is said to be tens of thousands, but according to those who know the inside story, it is probably no more than ten thousand. Since suppression has failed, we will seek appeasement. The way to appease is to reorganize or dismiss them. This should be discussed separately according to the situation of each part. However, if they can safely comply, serve the country, and defend the people, then reorganization may not be impossible. However, how will the leader, such as Li Jichun, be dealt with so that he will not cause more trouble? Therefore, only when the method of Li Jichun is determined will the county magistrate be able to take over after the Japanese troops withdraw. This is another important task that the committee should carry out at the same time.

After the great chaos, the people are extremely devastated. The public security in various places is very important. Moreover, these nineteen counties are not allowed to station troops, and the banditry must be prevented. Since there is no military agency, everything is in the administrative aspect. The official who is close to the people is the county magistrate. Therefore, the provincial government has selected capable and virtuous people to serve as county magistrates. These nineteen counties will be taken over. During the takeover and after the takeover, there must be special attention. The takeover personnel should guide them separately so as not to disrupt the overall plan due to small impatience, causing more suffering to the people and causing disputes. Therefore, the takeover committee is also an important task to guide the county magistrates in the special circumstances and special environments of these nineteen counties (June 29, Xiao).

Disasters of Great Floods in Various Counties of Jiangxi Province 90

Yongxiu, Hukou, and Xin Jian Counties are the Most Severe

Nanchang Communication. Continuous rain and mountain floods have caused the rivers in Jiangxi to rise sharply at times. According to the report of the hydrological station, the water level is only seven inches lower than the highest water level in the twentieth year. Fortunately, the dikes and embankments in various places have been built firmly in advance, and no major disasters have occurred. Since the water from the Yangtze River flowed back into Poyang Lake, the lake water flowed into the tails of the Ganfu Rivers, and the water勢 was rising against the stream, and the floodwater was larger than the upper water, so the upstream areas such as Xingan, Qingjiang, Fengcheng, and the southern part of Nanxin were not affected by the disaster, while Nanchang, Jiujiang, Poyang, Hukou, Zhangshu, Yongxiu, Dean, Wanzai, and other counties have been flooded in many places, especially Yongxiu, where the collapse産 is the largest. Xinjian and Hukou counties are the second largest, and Poyang is still struggling to rescue them. In Jiujiang along the river, Longkai River, Sanma Road, and Dazhong Road have also been flooded. The Water Conservancy and Water Conservancy Bureau has dispatched flood control personnel to carry materials such as cash, wooden piles, sacks, and torches to various counties for rescue. The disaster situation in the counties with heavier water disasters is recorded on the left.

Yongxiu County has become a country of Ze, and the Qingzhu, Liaofang, Yongshou, and other dikes in the second district, the Makou, Yangsi, Xiayang, and other dikes in the third district, and the Baijing Dike in the sixth district, a total of more than 20 dikes, have been flooded with more than 100,000 acres of farmland, and countless houses and livestock have been washed away. After several days and nights of rescue, the Sanjiao, Guodong, and Yongxing dikes were fortunately preserved, but they have not been completely out of danger. The current water势 is very large, only a foot lower than the amount of water in the twentieth year. The Yongwu road stone work has been completed eight or nine, and the Ma灣 and Baicha sections are too low, and the soil has been cultivated by more than ten feet, and they have been submerged. The repairs have just been completed, and they have been washed down again.

The lake water overflows all over Hukou Lake, and the gates of the county seat are all sealed by water. Small boats are on the streets, and the water depth is more than three feet. The houses inside and outside the ground floor have been flooded. The terrain in the countryside is lower, and most of them have been flooded. In Jiujiang, Baixi, Jiaoshan, Qingni, Fanyi Tangmai, Caijia, Yangjia, and other dikes in Poyang County have collapsed one after another, and even the area near the city river street has become a country of Ze. It is still increasing sharply in recent days and has invaded the main street. In addition to ordering the dike construction committee to send people to various dikes to carry out surveys and ordering the dikes to try to remedy them, the county authorities are selecting places to settle the victims, ordering the police to strictly prevent the Red bandits from taking the opportunity to disturb them, and issuing a notice to merchants not to increase the price of rice to maintain the food supply of the people.

Memorial Service Held in Baoding 91

The Venue is Tragic and Solemn

The Military and Civilians Mourn the National Trauma

Baoding Communication. After many days of preparation, the memorial service for the fallen soldiers who died in the Anti-Japanese War was held yesterday (the 25th) at the Lotus Pond Theater. About 4,000 people from military, political, police, institutions, groups, schools, and private individuals in the city participated. The details are recorded below.

At the entrance of the venue, there are military police maintaining order. The layout inside the venue is tragic and solemn. The surroundings are full of elegiac couplets, wreaths, and sacrificial flags from all walks of life. Jiang Zhongzheng's elegiac couplet says, "The righteousness is left in two simple, and the sincerity has been used to destroy the enemy. The loyal soul has been fought in hundreds of battles, and I hope that it can fly away and become mountains and rivers." Qian Dajun's elegiac couplet says, "Like your great integrity and loyalty, life is not vain, and death is also without regrets. I wish the country would lie down and taste the eternal remembrance of the martyrs. Don't let down today and wish the commander's elegiac couplet says, "The great ambition will not return, and the sacrifice for the country is without regrets. The great revenge has not been avenged, and the people are rescued from fire and water. Can the residual life have a time to rest?" The elegiac couplet of the Garrison Headquarters says, "Strive for independence for the country and strive for survival for the nation. You gave your lives to become benevolent, leaving a good name to be admired. Let us clear out the Communist Party and execute the traitors. I will inherit the legacy and will take back the lost land." The elegiac couplet of the Supplementary Soldiers Training Office says, "The more I add sorrow to the mourning, the more I hear the shouts and charges, regardless of the bursting brains and liver, and the flowing red blood. There is no other strategy for revenge, only sacrifice and struggle. The traces are last year in Shanghai and this year in the Great Wall."

After the participating groups of military police arrived, the meeting began at about 9 o'clock. First, play the elegy, then pay the last salute to the fallen soldiers, and be silent for five minutes for the fallen soldiers. Secondly, the chief priest Qian Dajun read the sacrificial text, and the representative of the preparatory committee read the sacrificial text. Then, Qian Dajun, the director of the Baoding camp, delivered a speech, saying that this unconditional invasion of Japan not only violated the peace of the international treaty but also violated human nature too much. Under our unbearable circumstances, we had to take up arms and defend ourselves. Everyone knows that the weapons of the Japanese army are more sophisticated than ours, and the military supplies are very sufficient. Last winter, our generals fought fiercely in the enemy's fierce artillery fire, starving and enduring the cold, and fighting each other. Although the weapons are not as good as them, the spirit is not weaker than the enemy. This shows that our conscience is not dead, and our ambition still exists. The fallen soldiers were able to sacrifice for the existence of the country and the personality of the nation. The greatness of their personality and the greatness of their spirit will be passed down to thousands of years. Then, Zhang, the representative of the Preparatory Committee of the Memorial Service for the Fallen Soldiers, delivered a speech, saying that in this war, Japan ignored everything, fish and meat in North China, and came to invade with violence and barbarity. The past facts are known to everyone. I have repeatedly questioned the facts of the invasion in the international community, waiting for a public solution. Unexpectedly, after the determination, Japan was still unrepentant and became more and more rampant, harassing North China and coveting Tianjin. We were forced to resist and defend ourselves. However, this anti-Japanese war is related to the survival of the country and the nation, and we should work together with one heart, do our best, and divide our work and cooperate. Now that the martyrs have been the vanguard for the people, resisting the strong and sacrificing their lives for the country, their responsibility has been fulfilled. The part left behind should be borne by everyone. We mourn the fallen soldiers. How can we not disappoint their hard work in the future? Finally, representatives from Commander Zhu, the 3rd Cavalry Regiment, and the 19th Route Army Suiying School gave speeches in turn. The meeting ended at 12 o'clock with slogans (26th).

Hunan Province's Extreme Austerity Measures 92

Cutting a Large Number of Institutions and Wasteful Expenses

Saving Over One Million Yuan Annually

Changsha Correspondence: Since the abolition of consolidated taxes, Hunan Province's finances have become increasingly difficult. With the outbreak of the September 18th Incident, all industries have declined, tax revenues have fallen short, grain prices have plummeted, and rural areas have gone bankrupt. Consequently, the situation has become even more dire, a condition rarely seen in the past decade or two. Party and government expenses have been allocated every ten days in recent years, with only 10% being disbursed each time. Since June, this has changed to every half month, with only 15% being disbursed each time. As of June 15th, only 10% of the November expenses from last year had been allocated. In total, arrears in political expenses will reach eight months, and future difficulties are inevitable. This year's budget for the 22nd year of the Republic for local income and expenditure in the province estimates annual expenditures at over 15 million yuan, while income, excluding the fictitious figure of 2.5 million yuan in public bonds, is less than 10 million yuan. He Jian then proposed implementing extreme austerity measures. In early June, this was presented to the provincial affairs meeting. At that time, committee members had many concerns due to excessive cuts, and advocated that everyone should share the burden. They suggested that all institutions should not be abolished, but that party and government expenses should be temporarily reduced by 30% to provide relief. However, after comprehensive calculation, even with a 30% reduction, the income and expenditure were still short by more than one million yuan. Therefore, at the provincial affairs meeting on the 20th, He again proposed implementing austerity measures, which were passed as proposed, to be implemented from July 1st. In total, 1,125,183 yuan will be saved annually, allowing income and expenditure to be balanced. The various items to be cut are listed below: (1) The Provincial Government's Fifth Section, with annual expenses of 31,368 yuan, will be abolished, with the Secretariat assigning personnel to handle its duties concurrently. (2) The salaries and expenses of statistical personnel in various counties, with annual expenses of 72,960 yuan, will be abolished. A clerk will be designated within the county government to handle statistics. (3) The Fourth Section of the Department of Civil Affairs, with annual expenses of 33,492 yuan, will be abolished. (4) The Autonomous Region Preparatory Committee, with annual expenses of 27,714 yuan, will be abolished and merged into the Department of Civil Affairs. (5) Temporary funding for promoting local autonomy, with annual expenses of 10,000 yuan, will be deleted. (6) Internal affairs inspection fees, with annual expenses of 15,000 yuan, will be deleted. (7) The Opium Prohibition Committee, with annual expenses of 19,553 yuan, will be abolished and merged into the Department of Civil Affairs. (8) The Nanyue Library, with annual expenses of 6,137 yuan, will be abolished and merged into the Nanyue Administration Bureau. (9) The Zhongshan Daily, with annual expenses of 56,160 yuan, will be abolished and merged into the National Daily. (10) Subsidies to the Dagong Bao, Quanmin Daily, and Shimin Daily, each at 19,200 yuan annually, and subsidies to the Wanwan Bao, Xiangjiang Wanbao, Hunan Wanbao, Bao, Pili Bao, and Xiangke Pictorial, each at 4,800 yuan annually, subsidies to the Nanjing Qingbai Bao, at 10,800 yuan annually, subsidies to the Nanjing Minli Bao, at 7,200 yuan annually, subsidies to the Nanjing Minzhi Review Society, at 9,600 yuan annually, subsidies to the Shiye Zazhi Society, at 1,200 yuan annually, subsidies to the Jiaotong Congbao Society, at 2,400 yuan annually, and subsidies to the Minsheng Xunkan Society, at 2,400 yuan annually, will all be stopped. (11) Other expenses subsidized to various newspapers from special funds, with unspecified annual amounts, will all be stopped. (12) The Finance Committee, with annual expenses of 20,022 yuan, will be abolished. (13) The Fifth Section of the Department of Finance, with annual expenses of 47,592 yuan, will be abolished. (14) The provincial tax collection bureaus in various counties, with annual expenses of 254,975 yuan, will be abolished. Only one accountant will be established within each county government to assist the county magistrate in handling provincial tax accounting matters, with an annual allowance of 30,240 yuan. (16) Various lake and grassland offices, with annual expenses of 22,347 yuan, will be abolished. (17) The Hengshan Silver Mine Village exploration project initiation fee, with annual expenses of 5,576 yuan, will be deleted. (18) The Lilin Model Pottery Factory maintenance fee, with annual expenses of 984 yuan, will be deleted. (19) Weights and measures expenses, with annual expenses of 5,520 yuan, will be deleted. (20) The Construction Special Committee, with annual expenses of 14,760 yuan, will be abolished. (21) The Highway Supervision Committee, with annual expenses of 13,092 yuan, will be reduced by 5,819 yuan. (22) The Education Design Committee, with annual expenses of 8,640 yuan, will be abolished. (23) The Vocational Education Committee, with annual expenses of 8,544 yuan, will be abolished. (24) The Primary Education Research Committee, with annual expenses of 10,080 yuan, will be abolished. (25) The 2234th Provincial Government Guard Team, with annual expenses of 125,153 yuan, will have two teams removed, reducing expenses by 62,577 yuan. (26) The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, with annual expenses of 580,878 yuan, will be reduced by 190,878 yuan. (27) Subsidies to the public security bureaus in various counties, with annual expenses of 122,400 yuan, will be halved to 61,200 yuan. (28) The Security Command's expenses, with annual expenses of 180,383 yuan, will be reduced by 14,976 yuan. (29) The Provincial Relief Committee, with annual expenses of 26,700 yuan, will be reduced by 5,340 yuan. (30) The coal expenses for the Yangtze River patrol armored ships, with annual expenses of 25,296 yuan, will be reduced by 10,416 yuan. (32) The Changsha Customs' levy for dike construction, with annual expenses of 5,436 yuan, will be reduced by 480 yuan. (33) The Yuezhou Customs' levy for dike construction, with annual expenses of 4,512 yuan, will be reduced by 240 yuan. In total, 1,125,183 yuan will be reduced, with a monthly reduction of over 90,000 yuan. (June 21st)

Suzhou Debt Collection Leads to Murder 93

Li Jusheng, a farmer near Zhangjiaqiao Town, Mudu Township, is over thirty years old and addicted to gambling, resulting in a heavy debt burden. Yesterday (the 1st), a creditor, Shi Shunnian, demanded repayment of 120 yuan from Li Jusheng. Li had no money to repay, and Shi insisted on collecting the debt, leading to a conflict. Li Jusheng, relying on his brute strength, used an iron rod to injure Shi Shunnian, striking a vital area. Within an hour, Shi died from his injuries. Li, realizing the consequences, immediately fled without a trace. The victim's family has requested that the authorities investigate the matter.

Chen Jifang, the young daughter of Zhengmao Dyeing Shop on Taoxing Bridge in this city, was lured and raped by Liu Gouzi, a dyer from Nanjing, at her sister Xia's residence at the Gexianweng Temple, causing serious injuries. It is now known that the suspect Liu Gouzi secretly returned from outside the South Gate yesterday and was discovered by patrol officer Wang Guohua of the Second Precinct Police Station. He was immediately arrested and taken to the County Public Security Bureau for preliminary interrogation. He confessed to being 20 years old, previously working as a dyer, but currently unemployed and residing at his sister Xia's house. His testimony was extremely cunning. The bureau, noting that the case had already been thoroughly investigated by the prosecutor's office, immediately prepared a document to transfer him to the prosecutor's office for investigation and handling.

Villagers in Tinglin Robbed 95

The home of Qiu Yinkun in the Eighteenth District of Tinglin was suddenly attacked by over ten bandits on the night of June 28th. They broke down the door and entered to loot. The owner's wife, realizing the situation was dire, climbed out of the back window to a neighbor's house. Elderly Virgin Commits Suicide by Drowning in Changshu 96

Shen Peiqi, the former Director of the Yuyu Bureau of this county, had a sister named Peizhen, who is currently 38 years old. She has strange quirks and has been a vegetarian since childhood. Relatives and friends have proposed marriage for her, but she has always refused. Therefore, approaching forty, she is still a virgin. Before her brother Peiqi became the Director of the Education Bureau, Peizhen often provided for him. Two years ago, Peiqi became an editor at the Shanghai Zhonghua Book Company and separated from his sister. Peizhen lived alone in the Shen family ancestral hall on North Gate Street in this county. However, recently, her behavior changed drastically. She constantly chanted Buddhist scriptures and frequently talked about committing suicide. Her cohabiting shoemaker tried to persuade and monitor her. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 30th, Peizhen threw herself into the well behind the ancestral hall. People went to draw water and discovered her body. They immediately rescued her, but she had been dead for some time. Her relatives in Shanghai have been notified to urge Shen Peiqi to return and arrange for her burial.

Yangtze River Water Level Rises in Yangzhou 97

The Yangtze River water level has suddenly risen in recent days. The Canal Works Bureau reported yesterday (the 30th) that the water level in Qingjiang has risen to one zhang seven chi two cun, Yumatou in Gaoyou to seven chi six cun, and the Sanyugou Lock in Jiangdu to one zhang two chi, a rise of several cun compared to the previous few days. Residents along the canal are quite worried.

Qiantai Money Shop Goes Bankrupt 98

Yangtai Money Shop Goes Bankrupt

Since the abolition of the tael and the adoption of the yuan in Yangzhou, the financial situation has become increasingly bleak, and many shops have closed. The Qiantai Money Shop, located at the Fengji Alley entrance on South Pi Street, has been operating for nearly thirty years and had a good reputation. Unexpectedly, it suddenly announced its closure on the 29th, engaging lawyer Zhu Naigeng to liquidate the accounts. It is said that deposits amount to approximately 60,000 yuan, mostly small deposits from ordinary citizens and many school personnel, which cannot be recovered, leading to the bankruptcy.

Ningbo Bandits Loot Shepan Town 99

Shepan Town in Ninghai County, Taizhou Prefecture, is located on the coast with a dense population and convenient transportation, making it prone to development. However, on the morning of the 27th of this month, over thirty bandit ships suddenly arrived with over three hundred bandits, armed with handguns, Mauser pistols, quick-firing rifles, and hand grenades. They landed in a secluded area near the town and first raided the town's defense corps, seizing all twenty-four firearms and over two thousand rounds of ammunition. After seizing the weapons, they proceeded to loot house by house, with no one spared. The bandits occupied the town for a full day, shooting and wounding six defense corps members during the looting. Before leaving, they kidnapped thirteen people, including the town head Ren Yongcan. Upon receiving the report, County Magistrate Wu Dingren immediately dispatched a large contingent of basic troops to suppress the bandits. He also used a long-distance telephone to report the emergency to the Ningbo Administrative Commissioner's Office, requesting that offshore patrol ships be mobilized.

Local News

Central Mint's New Currency Released Yesterday, Circulation Begins on the Fourth 100

Inspection Committee Announces Chemical Test Results Yesterday

Secretariat and Chemical Testing Departments Established with Separate Divisions

The new currency minted by the Central Mint was released yesterday. The New Currency Inspection Committee held a standing committee meeting at the Central Bank at 10:00 AM to announce the results of the chemical tests on the new currency, determining that it would be put into circulation on the market starting on the 4th. Details are as follows:

The standing committee meeting of the New Currency Inspection Committee was held at 10:00 AM yesterday on the third floor of the Central Bank. Attendees included Kong Xiangxi and Chen Jian'an of the Central Bank, Li Fusun of Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Mackay of Citibank, Spilman of the International Savings Society, and Hoshimin of HSBC. Bei Songsun of the Bank of China was absent due to leave. Secretary Li Junyao was present. Chairman Kong Xiangxi reported on the establishment of the secretariat, chemical testing department, and the process of inspecting the new currency. Discussions then began, resolutions were made, and the results of the chemical tests on the new currency's fineness and weight were announced, concluding at 11:30 AM.

Chemical Test Results: The Central Mint Inspection Committee issued Announcement No. 1 yesterday, stating, "Regarding the matter of announcing that the Central Mint has submitted the minted new currency to the committee for chemical testing in accordance with regulations, the committee appointed chemical tester Ge Laide to conduct continuous testing. According to the chemical tester's report on June 30th, the fineness and weight of the chemical test conform to the Silver Standard Coinage Regulations. In addition to issuing certificates No. 1 to No. 621 for the 3,105,000 yuan of silver standard coins that have already been inspected, this announcement is hereby issued." Chairman of the Central Mint Inspection Committee, Kong Xiangxi.

Two Department Organizations: The inspection committee has established a secretariat and a chemical testing department, located on the second floor of the Central Mint. The secretariat is temporarily managed concurrently by Li Junyao, secretary of the Central Bank, and is divided into four divisions: Audit Division, headed by Xin; Document Division, headed by Li MianTing; Affairs Division, headed by Yang Duo; and Deliberation Division, headed by Wang Debo. The chemical testing department's public tester is Ge Lander, a currency system consultant to the Ministry of Finance, and is divided into two divisions: Chemical Testing Division, headed by Cheng Yingzhang; and Inspection Division, headed by Yao Bailong. Each division has clerks.

Assessment of Factory Affairs: After the establishment of the inspection committee's secretariat, in accordance with Article 5 of the Inspection Regulations, the committee will begin assessing factory affairs and reviewing accounts starting this month. In accordance with Article 11, the Central Mint will submit its monthly accounting and expenditure reports to the inspection committee at the end of each month. The committee's audit division will handle the assessment and review.

Inspection Regulations: After the establishment of the inspection committee's chemical testing department, in accordance with the provisions of the Inspection Regulations, the committee will conduct chemical tests on the new currency and begin issuing it on July 1st. The factory bars minted by the Central Mint will be inspected by the chemical testing department in accordance with Article 9 of the Inspection Regulations. Those that meet the legal fineness and weight standards will be stamped with a certificate by the chemical tester. In accordance with the Inspection Regulations, the Central Mint will submit the number of new coins and factory bars minted each day, as well as the names and quantities of the silver and copper used, to the inspection committee for review.

Ma Zhanshan Reports on Meeting with Chiang Kai-shek in Jiangxi 101

Ma Stays in Shanghai Temporarily to Handle Aftermath

Hopes for National Unity

Visits Mr. Ma Xiangbo in the Afternoon

General Ma Zhanshan, the newly appointed member of the Military Affairs Commission, returned to Shanghai from Jiangxi. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, he met with reporters from various newspapers at the Huizhong Hotel on Hankou Road. Mr. Ma stated that he would be staying in Shanghai for about a month to handle the aftermath of his subordinates and returning refugees. Afterwards, he may travel north. He also recounted his trip to Jiangxi to meet with Chiang Kai-shek and his future positions and intentions. A detailed account of Mr. Ma's conversation follows:

Meeting with Chiang: Mr. Ma first stated, "I went to Jiangxi this time to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, first to report on the past situation in the Northeast, and second to discuss the handling of the aftermath of my subordinates. The results were quite satisfactory. Chairman Chiang has decided to first report all the brigades under my command to the central government, which will send personnel to Beiping to inspect them. Then, the troops will be reorganized. Secondly, an investigation will be conducted on the refugees and their families entering the pass, and a report will be submitted to the central government to seek relief. Most of the refugees and their families entering the pass are living in Shanghai, Beiping, and Xinjiang. I have already sent personnel to Beiping to investigate the exact numbers and whether the heads of the families are still alive, have been killed in action, or have been injured. The investigation in Shanghai has also begun. In Xinjiang, I have sent Brigadier General Wu Delin to inspect." Unchanged Anti-Japanese Stance: "During this trip to Jiangxi, I observed that the spirit of the Communist suppression military was very good. It will not be difficult to suppress the Jiangxi bandits. Regarding the anti-Japanese issue, my stance remains unchanged. I will listen to the central government's orders. However, anti-Japanese resistance requires adequate preparation and a comprehensive plan, so it is different from Communist suppression. Therefore, future anti-Japanese work should continue to focus on cultivating strength."

No Intention to Lead Xinjiang: "Regarding the rumors that I will be appointed chairman of the Xinjiang Provincial Government, Chairman Chiang did mention this issue to me in Nanchang. However, because the aftermath of my subordinates needs to be handled urgently, I did not express any opinion. As for the central government's appointment of me as a member of the Military Affairs Commission, I only saw it in the newspapers and have not received a formal appointment. But my personal aspiration is to continue the anti-Japanese cause and remain true to my original intentions. I have no intention of taking on other political duties at the moment."

Regarding Feng Yuxiang: When reporters asked about his thoughts on Feng Yuxiang's recent actions in Zhangjiakou, Ma said, "I absolutely sympathize with Mr. Feng's anti-Japanese stance. My stance has always been to advocate for anti-Japanese resistance, so we can be said to be standing on the same front. However, if someone uses the name of anti-Japanese resistance but has other intentions, then I certainly cannot agree. People's hearts are different, just like their faces, and it is impossible to know. As for Deng Wen and Li Haiqing, I have not received reports on the situation in Chahar, so I cannot speculate."

Impressions of the War Zone: "After returning to Shanghai, I visited the war zones of Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong. I deeply felt the cruelty of the Japanese army, which is even more brutal than what they inflicted on the Northeast. The devastation is great and the pain is deep. The Northeast and the Battle of Shanghai both demonstrate the enemy's brutality, making them enemies of the world. However, in terms of our country's losses, Shanghai's buildings were completely destroyed due to its urban nature, while the people of the Northeast were massacred. The enemy's brutality is the same."

Not Going to Southeast Asia: "The reports in the newspapers that I will be going to Southeast Asia to raise funds are inaccurate. When I was in Nanchang, I spoke with Mr. Xu Shiying about relief for Northeast refugees and other relief situations. I mentioned that I would like to serve charitable causes in the future, so that is where the rumors came from. But it does not mean that I will personally go to Southeast Asia to raise funds."

India as a Cautionary Tale: Mr. Ma concluded his responses to reporters by expressing his hope that the divide between the Southwest and the central government could be resolved quickly. "Because we are in a dangerous period of national crisis, we should quickly unite and thoroughly awaken to find a way to save ourselves. When I returned to China from Europe, I had a feeling while passing through India. India is also a large nation, similar to us. However, after India's subjugation, its internal strife still exists. Compared to China's current situation, there is a similar danger. Therefore, I believe that everyone should thoroughly awaken to the divide between the Southwest and the central government, so that there is hope for the country's future. Otherwise, we may not be able to avoid following in India's footsteps."

Staying in Shanghai Temporarily: Mr. Ma also stated, "My only task during this return to Shanghai is to handle the aftermath of my subordinates. Therefore, I will be staying in Shanghai for about a month to focus on handling the aftermath. After it is completed, I may travel north. Su Bingwen has gone to Hangzhou to visit his wife and children and has not yet determined when he will return to Shanghai."

Visiting Ma Xiangbo: After lunch yesterday, at 12:45 PM, Mr. Ma, accompanied by Zhang Dianjiu, went to Mr. Ma Xiangbo's residence on Xujiahui Road to visit the 94-year-old. He expressed his gratitude to Mr. Ma for his previous comments and spiritual support during the anti-Japanese resistance in the Northeast. The three men spoke for about an hour. Mr. Ma gave a detailed account of the anti-Japanese situation, and Mr. Ma praised his heroic patriotism. They took a photo together to commemorate the occasion. After leaving, Mr. Ma and Zhang turned to the French Concession to visit Yang Hu, talked for about half an hour, and returned to his residence after a brief walk in the Hardoon Garden at three o'clock.

Representatives of Merchants and Residents of North Sichuan Road Request Mediation by Councillors Shi, Yu, and Wang Yesterday Regarding the House Tax Case 105

Declaration Released Yesterday

Guowen News Agency: The entire merchant and resident community of the North Sichuan Road extraterritorial road extension, due to Councillors Shi Liangcai, Yu Qiaqing, and Wang Xiaolai of the Municipal Council also being executive and supervisory committee members of the Citizens' Federation, and having connections with both parties, believed that they could properly mediate the house tax issue. Therefore, at 3:00 PM yesterday, they elected representatives Chen Jiufeng, Wei Langxuan, Li Zifeng, Guan Jichuan, and Hu Zhaoying to visit Shi and Yu at the Shenbao and Navigation Club to present the situation and request them to serve as mediators. However, they did not meet them. It is reported that they will visit them separately this morning.

The entire merchant and resident community of the North Sichuan Road extraterritorial road extension released a declaration yesterday regarding the request for a delay in the collection of house tax, stating, "Since the North Municipal Tax Collection Office abruptly began collecting house tax without legal procedures or public announcement, the details of the situation have been reported in the newspapers for the past two months. Recently, after reading several statements and talks from the office, we have been accused of resisting taxes, which is harming the citizens. Therefore, we must clearly refute and announce the truth to all citizens and compatriots at home and abroad. Since the day the North Sichuan Road began collecting taxes, the merchants, aware of past events and the devastating state of the market after the war, which has caused burdens to increase without decrease, have written to the Citizens' Federation, a local mass organization, asking the 25th District Branch to act as a mediator, repeatedly explaining the hardships of the North Sichuan Road and the need for a delay in the collection. However, the office director has taken a business-as-usual approach, ignoring right and wrong, and using the house number as the only reason, without examining past events or current difficulties. The citizens, having no other choice, jointly petitioned the municipal government to stop the collection and requested a delay, but there has been no response for two months. Recently, they have been accused of resisting taxes, disregarding the plight of the merchants in dire straits, and showing no understanding. Instead, they are resorting to compulsory enforcement, which is truly unacceptable. The numbering of Chinese houses on North Sichuan Road and the establishment of Chinese police posts were achieved by the masses after they automatically fought for them in 1927. This is the responsibility of the masses, and the house and tax are the obligations of the citizens. However, the masses' repeated requests for a temporary delay are not a sign of resistance. The market has been devastated after the war, which is obvious. Compared to the ratios of the Eight Character Bridge and Jiangwan, which burden is lighter and which is heavier? The authorities should investigate. Moreover, the financial bureau's claim of complete facilities is unfounded. The sanitation and police powers of North Sichuan Road are all in the hands of foreigners. The so-called complete facilities include damaged but unrepaired sidewalks and uninstalled street lights. Can this really be called complete? As for the claim that foreigners have also paid some, citing the Yunfei Automobile Company is even more laughable to those in the know. The Yunfei house number is 74 Donghongjiang Road. The supply of water and electricity is supported by facts, and there are also many who have already paid concession taxes. While the people should support the government, the government should also prioritize the well-being of the people. In short, the citizens' request is only for a delay in the collection, and there is absolutely no resistance to taxation. We hope the authorities will investigate carefully and believe that a wise government will not lightly believe one-sided claims and recklessly destroy the survivors of the disaster. That would be fortunate indeed."

The China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong Route Changes to a Three-Day Trial Flight 106

First Flight from Guangzhou to Shanghai on the 7th

Shanghai-Guangdong Inaugural Flight Expected to Take About Ten Days

The trial flight and inaugural flight dates for the new Shanghai-Guangdong route of the China National Aviation Corporation have been largely decided after discussions at the company's 20th shareholders' meeting the day before yesterday. Details are reported as follows:

The preparation for the three-day trial flight on the Shanghai-Guangdong route has been underway for a long time. The leasing of airport offices at each station and the installation of electrical equipment have been handled in stages by Director Nie Kaiyi and are now complete. Originally scheduled for daily trial flights, it was changed to a new aircraft trial flight on the third of this month after a report and discussion at the shareholders' meeting held the day before yesterday, stopping at Wenzhou and Xiamen, and then flying directly to Guangzhou.

After the aircraft arrives in Guangzhou on the 7th, it will not fly back immediately. Instead, it will fly from Guangzhou to Shanghai on the 7th for its inaugural flight, initially delivering mail and postponing passenger transport. The inaugural flight period from Shanghai to Guangzhou is expected to be about ten days. In the future, it is planned to have two round-trip flights per week, but the dates have not yet been determined. The company has now printed commemorative envelopes for the opening of the route, which are sold at the company and the Directorate General of Posts. A postmark will also be affixed by the post office at the time of the inaugural flight for commemoration.

Provisional Passenger Fares The provisional passenger fares for the Shanghai-Guangdong route are as follows: From Shanghai to Xiamen, a one-way ticket is 175 silver dollars, and a round-trip ticket is 305 silver dollars. From Shanghai to Guangzhou, a one-way ticket is 270 silver dollars, and a round-trip ticket is 470 silver dollars. The airport and office locations at each station are as follows: (1) Airports: Wenzhou, the water surface in front of the Texaco oil machinery at the West Gate; Xiamen, Danggang; Guangzhou, the river surface. (2) Offices: Wenzhou, inside the Texaco foreign firm at No. 8 Shiban Lane in the city; Xiamen, No. 28, East Gate of Zhongshan Park; Guangzhou, the YMCA on the Bund.

New Aircraft Test Flight The company believes that Shanghai-Guangdong air transport must arrive at the destination on the same day, and it is expected that there will be many passengers between the two places after the route opens. Therefore, after ordering two new Sikorsky aircraft with faster speeds, they were rushed for assembly. One aircraft has now been assembled. Yesterday at 4 p.m., a test flight was conducted, taking off from Longhua Airport, circling the city, flying steadily, and the results were very good.

The Implementation of the Regulations on Marking the Country of Origin of Imported Goods is Postponed 107

Originally Scheduled to Begin Yesterday

Now Changed to January 1 of Next Year

The Regulations on Marking the Country of Origin of Imported Goods, after being formulated and promulgated by our side, were originally scheduled to take effect yesterday. The Shanghai Customs had already received orders to prepare for the implementation procedures. However, foreign merchants from the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany in Shanghai believe that the implementation of these regulations is too hasty and that they have not been given adequate preparation.

The chambers of commerce of each country forwarded a request to our authorities, requesting a postponement of the implementation, so that they could have sufficient time to telegraph export merchants in their respective countries to comply with the marking procedures. According to Shanghai Customs news, after receiving letters from the British, American, and German chambers of commerce, the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce held a meeting and considered the requests of the merchants from various countries to be reasonable. Therefore, they have approved the request to postpone the implementation of the Regulations on Marking the Country of Origin of Imported Goods until January 1 of next year. In addition to issuing a notice to customs offices in various places to comply, they have also sent a letter to the chambers of commerce of various countries in Shanghai to inform them for their reference and compliance.

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has repeatedly consulted with the Shanghai Telephone Company regarding the abolition of the five-cent telephone charge.
