The Bureau of Social Affairs Holds a Cooperation Movement Propaganda Week 109

Lectures Were Given Yesterday at the YMCA and the People's Education Center

Yesterday was the anniversary of the World Cooperative Movement. The Shanghai Bureau of Social Affairs launched a Cooperation Movement Propaganda Week, holding lectures at the Sichuan Road YMCA and the Municipal People's Education Center. Details are reported separately as follows:

Guests attending the YMCA included Zhu Weiyao, representative of the municipal government, Xing Wan, representative of the municipal party headquarters, Lai Kewen, representative of the municipal education bureau, Li Mo, representative of the public security bureau, Yu Zhenhui and Wu Xiaojiu of the municipal farmers' association, Wang Bingquan of the Shanghai Cooperative Enterprise Advancement Association, guests from all walks of life Wang Shiying and Zou Bingwen, and more than 100 employees of the Bureau of Social Affairs.

Chairman's Report Chairman Wu Xingya (replaced by Zhang Binghui) reported that today is the International Cooperative Movement Anniversary. The origin of this anniversary is that the International Cooperative Alliance stipulated in 1923 that a grand propaganda campaign should be held every year on July 1 to promote the true meaning of cooperation and that this day should be the International Anniversary Day for universal promotion around the world. Therefore, today is the most welcome and encouraging day for cooperative members in various countries and is also the most meaningful day in cooperation. In 1929, the central government stipulated measures for the Cooperative Movement Propaganda Week for the purpose of promoting cooperation, ordering provinces and cities to hold it to show their participation in the international cooperative movement. This year, the Bureau is holding an expanded propaganda campaign for the first time in Shanghai. As for the propaganda methods this time, (1) lecture meetings will be held at the People's Education Center and the Sichuan Road YMCA, and Mr. Pan Gongzhan is invited to give a radio broadcast lecture at the China Radio Station; (2) each newspaper will publish a special issue for the commemorative propaganda week today (currently, newspapers printing special issues include Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, Shishi Xinbao, etc.), using oral and written propaganda to popularize the true meaning of cooperation and attract the attention and understanding of the general public. Furthermore, while the propaganda of cooperation cannot be delayed, the promotion of facts is also an important plan. Therefore, the Bureau believes that the best way to arouse the special interest and deep understanding of the general public in cooperative societies is to create an experimental zone.

(Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Guest Speeches 110

After the chairman's report, guest Wang Shiying gave a speech entitled "The Relationship Between the Cooperative Movement and Social People," stating briefly: Today, I am here to participate in the Cooperative Movement Propaganda Week, and I will report to you on the meaning of cooperation that I have studied on weekdays. Our country has always paid little attention to the cooperative movement, and what our country needs most now is the promotion of cooperative enterprises. In today's world economic recession, cooperative enterprises are even more needed. In the past few years, the citizens of Shanghai have not had a sufficient understanding of this, so the National Government stipulated measures for the Cooperative Movement Propaganda Week in 1929, precisely because it has great significance. The Shanghai Bureau of Social Affairs is in charge, enabling capable people in society to jointly promote cooperative enterprises, not only in Shanghai but also to ensure that there are cooperative organizations in the interior. Citizens who do not understand believe that cooperative enterprises are very ordinary. In fact, if cooperative enterprises are carried out effectively, all agricultural products, such as transportation, will be done by themselves, so that capitalist merchants will have no way to suppress them. This is a peaceful revolutionary movement. Modern capitalism oppresses merchants and farmers, leading to the bankruptcy of the rural economy. Cooperative societies are to transform consumption and modern economic organization, and after overthrowing the old capitalism, the new economic organization will consolidate its strength on the old foundation. If farmers can understand this principle, then capitalists will collapse without being pushed. The organization of cooperative societies is for oneself on the one hand, and to help others on the other hand. At the same time, it is hoped that there will be a share of capital, that is, to contribute a share of capital. This kind of organization enables moral knowledge to have a considerable understanding, to do well, and there is also a kind of pleasure in the spirit. The development of cooperative enterprises in the countryside is the center of social interaction, part of it is for entertainment, and the vitality is also booming. Part of it focuses on education, and the people's knowledge can also develop accordingly. In today's era of internal and external troubles and the decline of people's livelihood, the cooperative enterprise can no longer be ignored. The speeches of Xing Wan and Zou Bingwen are omitted.

People's Education Center 111

Representatives included Li Suixian, Secretary of the Bureau of Social Affairs, Zhang Hanyun of the Municipal Party Department, Xu Xingjia of the Bureau of Health, Zhu Zhenxun of the Bureau of Education, Zhang Yichen of the Lih Jiao Hui [Likely a religious organization], Chen Peide of the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union, and employees of the Bureau of Social Affairs Chen Lengseng, Zhang Zhenyuan, Wang Gang, and guests from all walks of life Wu Juenong, Shi Boyan, etc., more than 200 people in total, chaired by Li Suixian.

After the opening ceremony and salutations, Chairman Li Suixian first reported that today is the International Cooperative Movement Anniversary, and the central government has stipulated measures for the Cooperative Movement Propaganda Week, so that the general public can have a general understanding. Zhejiang has already held 19 sessions, and we in Shanghai only started to carry it out last year. Due to the January 28 Incident, it was delayed until today. Although cooperative enterprises have been advocated, many people still do not understand the true meaning, so they cannot achieve considerable results. From this, we can see that the mission we bear today in holding the lecture meeting is very important. At the same time, it can make those who do not understand the truth and engage in the cooperative movement know that the cooperative enterprise is not an easy thing. The Bureau now employs experts and is starting to organize a cooperative enterprise research association. I also propose to organize a consumer cooperative society, which can make the cooperation of industrial and commercial enterprises tend to develop day by day. Rural cooperative societies are also the most important urgent task now. With rural cooperative societies, we can improve the rural self-governance and rural economy, because the national economy is based on the countryside. I am very grateful to the experts and various groups for participating in the preparation of this lecture meeting. However, due to the hurried preparation, everything is very simple, please forgive me.

Summary of Speeches Next, Zhang Hanyun, Zhang Yichen, and others gave speeches (lengthy speeches are not recorded). Then, Wu Juenong spoke on China's economic crisis and cooperative movements, briefly saying that due to economic panic and the dumping of foreign goods in recent years, imports exceed exports by about 500 million yuan every year in various industries, including agriculture, industry, and commerce. If cooperative enterprises are established, then the annual leak can be reduced or even cut off. Because China has never had such an organization, it is on the verge of economic bankruptcy. If we engage in cooperative enterprises, then production, consumption, sales, and distribution can also be improved, and the national economy can be restored, and the crisis can also be turned into safety. I hope that all sectors will work hard. Next, Shi Boyan spoke on the meaning of the cooperative movement, briefly stating that the difference between a cooperative enterprise and a Si Shang [likely means private/individual store] organization is that the cooperative society is not as financially strong as the company's capital. Because consumers and producers are directly connected, buying and selling from them is lower than the price of goods in stores, and the profits earned are given to the investors in part and to the shoppers in another part. At the same time, the amount of interest is determined according to the size of the customer's transaction. The power of the cooperative society is equal, and each person has the right to elect and be elected, which is not like a company whose power is determined by the number of shares. If a shareholder withdraws shares, the reason must be sufficient before they can withdraw, which is not like a company that can buy and sell at will. Next, Chen Peide and others gave speeches, which are also omitted. The meeting adjourned at 5:30 p.m.

The Society's Dinner Yesterday was the first day of the International Cooperative Movement Propaganda Week. Members of the China Cooperative Society and teachers and students of the Cooperative Research Class attached to the Society held a reunion dinner at Tongxinglou on Simalu at 7:00 p.m. A total of more than 40 members of the Society and students of the Research Class attended. At the beginning of the dinner, Wang Shiying, executive committee member of the Society, reported on the situation of the Society over the past five years and its current situation. Then, Wu Juenong, director of academic affairs of the Research Class, reported on the process of running the class. Li Quanshi, Wu Huanru of the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, and representatives of the Research Class students also gave speeches. Finally, there were recreational activities, which were very grand for a while.

The Revised and Approved New Articles of Association of the Hanyeping Company 113

A Total of Six Chapters and Thirty-Seven Articles

The Hanyeping Coal and Iron Ore Joint Stock Co., Ltd. convened an extraordinary shareholders' meeting on the afternoon of June 30 to discuss and amend the company's articles of association. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is learned that a total of 310 shareholders attended the meeting that day, representing 77,080 people. According to the company, the actual paid-up capital is 373,325 shares, accounting for slightly more than one-fifth. The Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Communications are also shareholders of the company. Director Huang Jintao and Section Chief Wang Zhongwu represented the equity of each ministry to attend the meeting. As a result of the meeting, the revised articles of association, consisting of six chapters and thirty-seven articles, were approved. However, the number of attendees was insufficient, so the decision was made as a preliminary resolution in accordance with the law, and another meeting will be convened within one month to confirm the decision. The company's approved revised articles of association are recorded below:

Revised Articles of Association of Hanyeping Coal and Iron Ore Joint Stock Co., Ltd. 114

Chapter I: General Provisions Article 1: This company is formed by the merger of Hanyang Iron Works, Daye Iron Mine, and Pingxiang Coal Mine, and is named Hanyeping Coal and Iron Ore Joint Stock Co., Ltd. In accordance with the provisions of the Company Law for joint stock companies, the responsibility of the shareholders is limited to paying up their share capital. Article 2: The business scope of this company is as follows: (1) Mining iron ore, coal ore, and other ores such as magnesium, aluminum, manganese, and silicon required for smelting; (2) Smelting iron, refining steel, and manufacturing all kinds of building materials, agricultural tools, and industrial equipment with steel; (3) Burning and refining coke, bricks, tiles, cement, and other materials; (4) Transportation and sales of mineral products and manufactured goods; (5) Other related ancillary industries. Article 3: The mining operations of this company shall be carried out in accordance with the Mining Law. Other matters related to mining, such as laying railways, dredging rivers, building docks, navigating ships, and installing telecommunications, shall be handled in accordance with current laws and regulations. Article 4: The general office of this company is located in the urban area of Shanghai. Article 5: The announcements of this company shall be published in two or more daily newspapers in the location of the general office. Chapter II: Shares Article 6: The total capital of this company is set at 20 million silver dollars, divided into 400,000 shares of 50 dollars each, all of which have been fully paid up. As of now, a total of 373,325 shares have been fully paid up, amounting to 18,666,250 silver dollars. Article 7: The shares are generally registered shares, issued by the chairman of the board and four or more other directors with their signatures and seals. Only nationals of this country can hold shares; otherwise, they are invalid. Article 8: Shares are divided into three types: first-class preferred shares, second-class preferred shares, and common shares. Article 9: Shareholders themselves and the representatives appointed in the name of a group or firm shall report their names, addresses, and seals to the company for record. The same applies to any changes; otherwise, the company shall not be responsible for any losses incurred. Article 10: When transferring shares, both the assignor and the assignee shall report to the company for verification and transfer. Before the transfer is completed, the company shall still recognize the original shareholder as the shareholder. Article 11: When a representative of a group or firm changes, the shareholder himself and the newly appointed representative shall declare to the company. Those who apply for changes due to inheritance shall provide sufficient evidence. The company may also order them to find a reliable guarantor when deemed necessary. Article 12: If a stock certificate is damaged or needs to be divided or combined, an application may be made to the company for replacement. However, if the damage is so severe that it is difficult to identify, the company may order the announcement in the newspaper or also order the finding of a reliable guarantor. 1. One to ten shares, each share has one right; 2. Eleven to one hundred shares, calculated at 70% discount, ignoring the remainder; 3. One hundred and one to five hundred shares, four shares are one right; 4. More than five hundred shares, five shares are one right. In each shareholders' meeting election, the three old directors with the most votes are retained first, and the remaining eight are elected by single non-transferable vote. Article 21: The chairman of the shareholders' meeting shall be the chairman of the board, but for extraordinary meetings convened at the request of the shareholders, the chairman may be elected by the shareholders. Article 22: Resolutions of the shareholders' meeting shall be passed by a majority of the voting rights of the shareholders present, with more than half of the total number of shares represented in attendance, except as otherwise provided in the Company Law. In case of a tie, the chairman shall decide. Article 23: Voting at the shareholders' meeting may be done by other methods besides voting, but if ten or more shareholders object to other methods or if there are doubts about other methods of voting, voting shall be used. Article 24: During the meeting period of the shareholders' meeting, the chairman may decide, or the chairman may announce an extension upon the vote of more than one-third of the voting rights of the shareholders present, if necessary, but the total shall not exceed three days. Article 25: The minutes of the shareholders' meeting shall be signed and sealed by the chairman and, together with the shareholders' attendance book and the power of attorney of the representatives, shall be kept by the board of directors in the company. Chapter IV: Staff Article 26: This company shall have eleven directors and four supervisors, all of whom shall be elected by the shareholders' meeting. However, a director shall have at least 300 shares and a supervisor shall have at least 100 shares to be eligible for election. After taking office, the directors shall hand over their shares as evidence of their election to the supervisors for safekeeping in the company. Article 27: The term of office of the directors is three years, and the term of office of the supervisors is one year. Both directors and supervisors may be re-elected. If the number of vacancies during the term reaches one-third, an extraordinary shareholders' meeting shall be convened immediately to elect replacements to fill the original term. If replacements have not been elected, the board of directors may, if deemed necessary, have the next most elected candidate perform the duties on their behalf. Article 28: The board of directors is organized and located in the company's general office and meets at least once a month to decide on important matters of the company. Article 29: Resolutions of the board of directors shall be passed by the presence of more than half of the total number of directors and the consent of more than half of the directors present. In case of a tie, the chairman shall decide. Article 30: The directors shall elect one chairman and two managing directors. The chairman executes all business and represents the company externally. The managing directors reside in the company and assist the chairman in executing business. If the chairman is unable to attend to duties, one of the managing directors shall be elected to act on his behalf. Article 31: Each supervisor may exercise the right of supervision independently. In addition to performing duties in accordance with the law, supervisors may also attend meetings of the board of directors and express opinions, but have no voting rights. Article 33: The salaries of the chairman and managing directors shall be determined by the board of directors, but shall be subject to the consent of the supervisors. Chapter V: Accounting Article 33: The accounts of this company shall be settled monthly at the end of each month, calculated once in June each year, and the total calculation once at the end of each year. The accounts for the total calculation period shall be prepared by the board of directors in various forms in accordance with the law and submitted to the supervisors for verification. After issuing the report, they shall be submitted to the annual shareholders' meeting for approval. Article 34: When calculating the total calculation, if there is a surplus after deducting total expenses and various depreciation reserves and labor rewards from the total income, one-tenth of it shall be set aside as public reserve, followed by dividends at 6% per annum. The remainder shall be allocated in the following proportions: 1. Shareholders' bonus: 200 parts; 2. Remuneration for the chairman, managing directors, directors, and supervisors: 15 parts; 3. Remuneration for office staff: 30 parts; 4. Labor welfare fund: 15 parts; 5. Special bonus for first-class preferred shares: 15 parts; 6. Special bonus for second-class preferred shares: 15 parts; 7. Special public reserve: 10 parts. Article 35: The distribution of profits shall be carried out after the resolution of the annual shareholders' meeting has been approved. Dividends and shareholders' bonuses shall be distributed according to the register of shareholders on the date of suspension of transfer. Chapter VI: Supplementary Provisions Article 36: All administrative regulations of this company shall be determined separately by the board of directors. Article 37: Matters not covered in these articles of association shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Company Law and the Mining Law. Any changes shall be resolved by the shareholders' meeting in accordance with the law and reported to the competent authorities for record.

Opposition to the New Tax System for the Tobacco and Liquor Industry 116

Yesterday, Repeated Submissions to Departments and Appeals

Seeking Assistance from the Chamber of Commerce and the French Municipal Council

The Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Liquor Industry Association, along with the five industry associations of Liang Baijiu, Local Yellow Wine, Shaoxing Wine, Soy Sauce Wine, and Soy Sauce Gardens, are in opposition to the Ministry of Finance and the Tax Affairs Administration's new fixed tax system, which abolished public sales and tax collection in the 22nd year, citing its harsh and cumbersome clauses and severe penalties. This has been previously reported. Yesterday, the association and others separately telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, the Tax Affairs Administration, and the Stamp Tobacco and Liquor Tax Bureau, appealing for revisions to the new regulations to ensure fairness. The original texts are excerpted below:

Tobacco Industry Submission The Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco Industry Association's submission to the Ministry of Finance's Tax Affairs Administration and the Stamp Tobacco Tax Bureau states: "To the Director of the Tax Affairs Administration of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing and the Stamp Tobacco Tax Bureau: We, the association, according to the opinions presented by Yu Xunlu, a representative from member tobacco industry associations in Yixing, Nanjing, Wuxian, Wujin, Danyang, Wuxi, Liuhe, Liyang, Jintan, Gaoyou, Dongtai, and Tongshan, concerning Article 2 of the special tax regulations for domestic tobacco, which stipulates a tax of four yuan, one jiao, and five fen in national currency per 100 jin (approximately 50 kg), are uncertain of the standard used. If considering cured tobacco, which is sourced from foreign merchants procuring high-quality tobacco leaves for curing and is a raw material for manufacturing premium cigarettes, with prices ranging from at least three to ten yuan per jin in national currency, while the price of domestically produced tobacco leaves and strands in the production area is only around two yuan per 100 jin for the majority. The selling price of the finished domestic tobacco strands is at most three to four jiao per jin. Given the disparity in selling prices, the quality of tobacco leaves should be differentiated. This article taxes all at four yuan, one jiao, and five fen per 100 jin, which is unfair. The regulations for collecting fees on tobacco leaves based on estimated value and tiered rates seem fairer. In recent years, cigarette sales have been brisk, while domestic tobacco strands are ignored, and business is declining daily. If Article 2 of the special tax is not amended, not only will domestic tobacco merchants be unable to bear the heavy tax burden, but also farmers in the production areas will have no outlet for inferior tobacco, which will have a significant impact on the national economy and people's livelihood. We request that your bureau forward this to the Ministry of Finance for review, to understand the situation, and to grade the estimated value into three levels, or set it as six yuan for Grade A, four yuan for Grade B, and two yuan for Grade C, and tax according to the grade, in order to ensure fairness and maintain the livelihoods of farmers and merchants." Upon review by our association, the opinions presented by the representatives accurately reflect the actual situation in various counties. Article 2 of the special tax regulations should be amended urgently. Furthermore, the representatives stated during their visit and petition that they were assured that the matter would be considered and handled accordingly. Therefore, we report this matter by telegram, hoping that you will review and revise it to maintain commerce and ensure fairness for the public good. The Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco Industry Association jointly submits."

Liquor Industry Submission 117

The five industry associations of Liang Baijiu, Local Yellow Wine, Shaoxing Wine, and Soy Sauce Gardens submit to the Tax Affairs Administration's Tobacco and Liquor Tax Bureau, stating: "Submitting this to report the dispatch of representatives to state the harshness of the new system and appeal for its abolition, hoping that you will review and adopt it to maintain commercial operations. We, the association, recently learned that the Tax Affairs Administration is abolishing public sales and tax collection in the 22nd year and establishing a new fixed tax system with harsh and detailed clauses and severe penalties. This not only increases the burden but also creates a dense web of laws, causing panic among liquor merchants. At the joint meeting of the association and others on the 29th of this month, it was unanimously agreed that the implementation of this new system would be tantamount to destroying commercial operations. If it is forcibly implemented, it will absolutely not be recognized, and we will insist to the end, sacrificing everything if necessary. It was resolved to each appoint two or one representative to jointly petition and appeal for its abolition. Zhu Shirong and Mei Weige from the Liang Baijiu industry, Fang Zhongheng and Jin Juqing from the Local Yellow Wine industry, Zhou Jinrong and Song Jinrong from the Shaoxing Wine industry, Han Xingwei from the Soy Sauce Wine industry, and Chen Weiwen and Song XingSui from the Soy Sauce Garden industry were publicly nominated as petition representatives, which was unanimously approved. We jointly submit this document, hoping that you will review it, adopt our humble opinions, abolish the new system to maintain commercial operations and avoid disputes, and we will be grateful. In addition to sending letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Liquor Industry Association for assistance, we respectfully submit this to Xie, the Director of the Tax Affairs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, and Liang Luo, the Director of the Jiangsu Stamp Tobacco and Liquor Tax Bureau."

Letter to the Chamber of Commerce, etc. 118

The five industry associations and the joint association write to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: "To the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: We are writing to inform you that we, the association, recently learned that the Tax Affairs Administration of the Ministry of Finance is abolishing public sales and tax collection in the 22nd year and establishing a new fixed tax system with harsh and cumbersome clauses and severe penalties. This not only increases the burden but also creates a dense web of laws, causing panic among liquor merchants. At the joint meeting of our association and others on the 29th of this month, it was unanimously agreed that the implementation of this new system would be tantamount to destroying commercial operations. If it is forcibly implemented, it will absolutely not be recognized, and we will insist to the end, sacrificing everything if necessary. It was resolved to each appoint two or one representative to jointly petition and appeal for its abolition and to send letters to the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Liquor Industry Association and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for assistance, which was unanimously approved. Previously, this case was raised as a temporary motion during the member conference convened by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and submitted to your esteemed organization for review and transfer. In addition to sending separate letters, we send this special letter, hoping that your esteemed organization will uphold justice and provide assistance, and swiftly strive to abolish it based on the situation to maintain commercial operations. We will be grateful. Addressed to the Nanjing Tobacco and Liquor Industry Association, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Letter to the French Municipal Council 119

A letter addressed to the Shanghai French Municipal Council states: "We are writing to inform you that, concerning the Ministry of Finance's Tax Affairs Administration's changes to the tobacco tax rates in the 22nd year, abolishing public sales and tax collection and establishing a new fixed tax system with harsh clauses and severe penalties, merchants in the concessions, who have been bearing heavy business license fees and paying minimal public sales taxes, are now facing a sudden increase in large amounts due to the new system. This not only increases the burden but also creates a dense web of laws, causing panic among merchants. At the joint meeting of our association on January 29th, it was unanimously agreed that the implementation of this new system would be tantamount to destroying commercial operations. If it is forcibly implemented, it will absolutely not be recognized, and we will insist to the end, sacrificing everything if necessary. We fear that the administration will stubbornly act alone, ordering the Suzhou-Zhejiang-Anhui Unified Tax Inspection Office to dispatch personnel to request your Bureau to dispatch police to intimidate, which will inevitably incite incidents. Who will bear the responsibility? Our association is preventing disasters before they happen and stopping harm from approaching. We are sending this special letter, hoping that your Bureau will investigate and consider that our industry has always fulfilled its obligation to pay liquor license fees. Before this case is resolved, if the Inspection Office requests the dispatch of police, please temporarily suspend assistance to alleviate the merchants' difficulties and avoid disputes. We would appreciate a reply to reassure us. We are grateful. Addressed to the Shanghai French Municipal Council."

Yang Xingfo's Funeral Today 120

The Academia Sinica and the Science Society of China

Held Public Memorial Services Separately Yesterday Morning and Afternoon

Yang Xingfo, the former Director-General of the Academia Sinica, who was assassinated, has been temporarily laid to rest at the International Funeral Home. The funeral will be held today, with burial at the Yong'an Cemetery. Yesterday morning and afternoon, colleagues from the Academia Sinica and the Science Society of China held separate public memorial services.

The Academia Sinica's public memorial service was held at 10:00 AM. Fu Sinian, Director of the Institute of History and Philology in Nanjing, Qian Tianhe, Director of the Natural History Museum, Gao Pingzi, Director of the Astronomical Institute, Xu Jifu, Secretary of the Academia Sinica, and Wang Yihou, Accountant, all came to Shanghai to participate, along with approximately two hundred staff members from the General Office and various institutes in Shanghai. Yang's family members were all present at the memorial hall to return the gestures of respect. The arrangement inside the hall was simple, with elegiac couplets presented by various circles hanging all over the walls, expressing deep sorrow. Flowers and wreaths were placed before the coffin, creating a very poignant scene. Cai Yuanpei, the President of the Academia Sinica, personally presided over the ceremony. The ceremony was very simple, consisting of bowing, reading the eulogy, and presenting the wreaths.

The Science Society of China's public memorial service was held at 3:00 PM, with all members of the society participating. Wang Liang, Director of the Institute of Northern Studies of the Academia Sinica, presided over the ceremony. Over thirty members of the society attended, including Peng Xuepei, Director of the Administrative Affairs Office of the Executive Yuan, Shen Yi, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, Li Zhaohuan, President of Jiaotong University, Cao Liangxia, President of Datong University, Hu Gangfu, a full-time researcher at the Physics Research Institute of the National Academia Sinica, and He Dekui, Secretary of the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Shanghai French Concession. The text of the society's eulogy is recorded below: "Alas, Mr. Yang, afflicted with lung disease, medicine always at your side, constantly fearing a short life. We worried about you, your ambition strong but your body weak, your melancholy harming your years, perhaps like Jia Yan. In recent years, you became stronger, always prepared for action. You served in Nanjing and Shanghai, flying high. The demon of illness startled you, at banquets and gatherings. Who would have thought that you would die so strangely, not from disease, not from old age, not on the battlefield. A chaotic gunfire, a lone car unable to move. A bullet pierced your heart, leaving a trail of blood. A bright and wise man, gone in an instant. Alas, alas! You lived in academic institutions, not seeking political power. You were concerned about prisoners and helped those in danger. Who would have thought that such a benevolent man would suffer such a great wrong. One night in the car, you left no last words. The joy of your enemies, the sorrow of those who loved you. What did you do to deserve this? The sharpest weapons were your pen and tongue, but you did not hide them deeply. Every inch of your flesh feels the pain. The beloved sword will never be seen again, the orphaned children will be separated forever. Where does your spirit go? Our hearts burn with grief. Alas, alas! Connected to this society, starting in America, then moving to Jinling, your reputation grew. The foundation was built, the summer house was erected, becoming a forest of knowledge, all thanks to your plans. Running around, planning, your tongue scorched, your mouth parched, enduring hardships, never changing from beginning to end. Every year at the society gathering, you resolved disputes, made yourself heard, guiding with your torch, awakening with your morning bell. From Zhejiang to Guangdong, from Hebei to Shandong, you connected people from all over the country. We looked forward to opening up Sichuan and Chongqing. But now our leader has fallen, what shall we do? Alas, alas! In this world, who does not die? To live out one's life is what the world praises. When Mingfu drowned, you were heartbroken. When Zhimo died, your tears flowed. You grieved for the talented who were not allowed to live long. It was not just mourning a friend, but harming the nation. You saw Hu and Xu die even more tragically. On the open road, a trap was suddenly set, no time to defend, no chance to shout. Your office was nearby, but now it's shrouded in darkness. Our friendship with you was like that of brothers. Within five steps, there was no way to help you. The flames of the enemy burned high, the voices of your relatives and friends were swallowed. We build this tomb, offering wine and sacrifices, remembering your friendship, but unable to comfort your wronged soul. Alas, alas! May you enjoy this sacrifice."

After the public memorial service, the "Dotting the Spirit Tablet" ceremony was held, presided over by Cai Yuanpei. Yang's young son, Xiaofo, was in the hall, looking deeply saddened. He returned the gestures of respect to all those who came to pay their respects over the past few days. However, due to his wound not yet fully healed and his weak health, he will need to be hospitalized for treatment and recovery after the funeral. The funeral will be held today at 3:00 PM, with burial at the Yong'an Cemetery. Before the funeral, all the guests will offer their respects, followed by the family members. The route will be from Jing'an Temple Road to Haig Road to Hongqiao Road, and then to Yong'an Cemetery on Hopeland Road for burial.

Shanghai Navigation Industry Establishes Shipping Friends Bank 121

Assisting in the Development of the Shipping Industry

Regulating the Finances of Shipping Friends

With the increasing number of shipping companies in Shanghai and the increasing number of shipping friends, there has been a lack of financial regulation mechanisms. Although the Maritime Accident Insurance Company was established this spring, it was only intended for the consolation and relief of sailors in distress, and there was no proper solution to the general economic problems. Now, initiated by shipping industry figures such as Jia Dingxi, Ren Ziqing, Shi Zupei, Shen Zhongyi, and Cao Zijia, the Shipping Friends Bank has been established, which will greatly benefit shipping friends and the shipping industry. The details are explored below:

Founding Personnel Many of the initiators are central figures in the shipping industry, including shipowners on various rivers and seas such as Shi Zupei, Sun Meihong, Cui Songgu, Fu Dexing, Chen Zixian, Zheng Luzhai, Feng Changxu, Zhao Ruosi, Gao Chenghang, Wu Huisheng, Feng Yuming, Mao Rucai, Zou Xipei, Wu Xifeng, and Xin Lixiang, totaling twenty-three people. Sun Hengfu, the General Manager of the Ningbo Commercial Bank, and Shen Zhongyi and Cao Zijia are also initiators and founders.

Origin and Declaration Since the start of trade between China and foreign countries, nearly a century has passed, and transportation has gradually increased, with the shipping industry becoming increasingly developed. It is noted that in coastal provinces and along the Yangtze River ports, there are countless ships and tens of thousands of shipping friends. Their business income and expenditure amount to over ten million yuan annually. There has been a lack of specialized banks to regulate their financial affairs, which has greatly affected their economy and prevented the full development of their business. Colleagues have recognized this and have organized the Shipping Friends Bank to regulate the industry's finances and support its development. A savings department will be established to facilitate savings for shipping friends. All measures are aimed at promoting the welfare of the shipping industry, mutual assistance, and mutual benefit. The bank will adopt a prudent approach, avoid speculation, and ensure stable operations and complete financial transparency. Shareholders can elect representatives to inspect the accounts at any time for supervision. The authorized capital is 500,000 yuan. Once the shares are fully subscribed, a founding meeting will be held, and applications will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry for approval and registration. The opening date will be announced in due course.

A Glimpse of the Contents The bank has been preparing for establishment by the founders, who have already subscribed to one-half of the shares. The proposed prospectus is as follows: (1) Name: Shipping Friends Bank. (2) Purpose: To promote savings among shipping friends and to protect the progress of the shipping industry. (3) Organizational Nature: To be organized in accordance with the new Banking Law promulgated by the National Government, handling commercial and savings operations. (4) Capital: Authorized capital of 500,000 yuan in national currency, divided into 10,000 shares at 50 yuan per share, to be paid in full at once. (5) Location: Shanghai. As business develops, branch offices will be established in other cities, or necessary agency offices will be established in other cities first. (6) Dividends: Weekly interest of eight percent, calculated from the date of payment of shares. (7) Shareholding: Those holding 30 or more shares will have the right to elect directors. (8) Plans: 1. Shipping friends can save money from one yuan upwards, with preferential interest rates. 2. Shipping friends can borrow small amounts from the bank, with detailed regulations to be formulated separately. For example, each ship friend can have the shipowner and chief mate endorse the loan and can also borrow advance wages from the bank. 3. Money saved in one bank can be withdrawn at the agent office of the bank in various places if needed, and the remittance fee can be waived for convenience. 4. When the bank has a surplus, it will allocate a certain amount to carry out shipping friends' public welfare activities. 5. Once the shares are fully subscribed, a shareholders' meeting will be convened to discuss the articles of association, submit them for registration, and then exchange the shares. 6. The share money will be collected by the Ningbo Commercial Bank and can only be used after the bank establishment procedures are completed. Before the procedures are completed, it cannot be used. 7. The initiators will first nominate a preparation director to set up a preparation office to carry out the work. The expenses will be minimized and advanced by the preparation director, and the expenses will be audited by the shareholders' meeting after the bank is formally established.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Tax on Imported Foreign Rice and Flour 122

To Save China's Declining Rural Areas

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, requesting a tax on imported foreign rice, foreign wheat, and foreign flour to save China's declining rural areas. The original petition states: "Submitting this petition. On June 25th, our association convened the fourth member representative assembly, where the Rice Milling Industry Association and the Rice Trading Industry Association proposed that domestic agricultural economies have been bankrupted due to continuous natural and man-made disasters in recent years. Last year, due to the massive import of foreign rice, while the price of all other goods rose, the price of rice alone was depressed to an extreme level, causing the livelihood of farmers, who make up 83% of the national population, to be on the verge of extinction. Taking this city as a densely populated area as an example, the consumption of food is huge, but rice merchants are suffering, and almost all of them cannot maintain their precarious existence. The situation of domestic agriculture and commerce is like this. Our country is founded on agriculture, and the prosperity or decline of the country depends on the stability of farmers' lives. It is not possible to ignore the fact that the consumers in the big cities, who account for a small percentage of the national population, benefit from cheap food. Although there may be a need for foreign rice to adjust supply and demand, the reorganization of the rural economy and the survival of farmers should be considered in both domestic and foreign contexts, so that they will not be bankrupted or endangered. In this severe period of agricultural and commercial decline, and for the sake of supply and demand, it is proposed to petition the Ministry of Industry to consult with the Ministry of Finance to impose countervailing duties on imported foreign rice, which will benefit the national treasury and assist farmers and merchants. Even if supply and demand reach a certain level, it may be possible to modify the measures at any time. In modern times, all countries implement tax protection policies for domestic agriculture, industry, and commerce in order to ensure domestic stability and external development. Today, the situation in our country requires the implementation of protection policies to save ourselves from danger. Therefore, we have described the difficult situation of agriculture and commerce in detail, hoping that you will make a decision as soon as possible." It was decided to petition your ministry to promptly handle the matter. It has been found that foreign rice, foreign wheat, and wheat flour from various countries are being dumped in our country due to overproduction, which harms the livelihood of farmers, causing the decline of rural production. Even the most prosperous provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang are not immune to this situation. The reports from the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways show a sharp decline in the transportation of agricultural products, which is alarming. In April of this year, our association intended to request the Grain Industry Association to separately levy import duties, and we petitioned your ministry, which forwarded it to the Ministry of Finance for review. Now, we are continuing to request its prompt implementation, which shows that the matter is urgent and cannot be ignored. We respectfully petition your ministry to review and handle the matter promptly for the public good."

Cracking Down on Water Adulteration in Rice 123

Rice merchants in this city have reported that some boatmen transporting rice are adulterating the rice with water in an attempt to increase the volume, causing significant losses to the rice merchants. Therefore, they petitioned the Bureau of Social Affairs to formulate measures to crack down on this practice. It is now learned that the measures have been drafted by the Bureau and forwarded to the Municipal Government for approval and promulgation. The original text is copied below: (Shanghai Municipal Measures for Cracking Down on Water Adulteration in Rice) Article 1: These measures shall be used to crack down on any boatmen who transport rice to the city and adulterate the rice with water in an attempt to increase the volume. Article 2: When a rice store or shop discovers that the rice transported by a boatman is suspected of being adulterated with water, it shall immediately report the boatman's name to the Bean and Rice Industry Association, which shall submit it to the Bureau of Social Affairs to dispatch personnel to supervise the inspection. Article 3: The Bean and Rice Industry Association shall designate representatives to be supervised by the Bureau of Social Affairs to identify whether the rice has been adulterated with water. The number of representatives from the Bean and Rice Industry Association shall be determined by the association. Article 4: If it is confirmed after identification that the boatman has adulterated the rice with water, the boatman shall be fined twenty yuan. The same shall apply to repeat offenders. If the boatman does not repent and commits the offense for the third time, in addition to being fined twenty yuan, the local Bean and Rice Industry Association shall notify the inland colleagues that the boatman shall never be allowed to transport rice again. Article 5: The Bureau of Social Affairs shall review and decide on the penalty stipulated in the preceding article. However, to avoid difficulties in enforcement, the boat shall be detained before the fine is paid, or the Public Security Bureau shall be requested to instruct the district office to detain it. Article 6: These measures shall be submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and promulgation.

Court Changes Office Hours 126

The Shanghai Special District First Court will slightly change its office hours every summer. This year, it will follow the same practice. Therefore, from yesterday, the office will open at 8:00 AM every day and close at 1:00 PM. All cases of arrest, public prosecution, and private prosecution will be heard during this time. The notice has been issued and posted by President Shen Jiayi.

The Jiangsu High Court Third Branch of the French Concession and the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special Court will, as usual, take a vacation in the afternoon due to the hot weather in the summer. The office hours will be changed from 8:00 AM to 1:00 PM daily from July 1st to August 31st. Liang Renjie and Ying Shi, the two presidents of the two courts, and Zhao Shibei and Chen Yan San, the two chief prosecutors, jointly issued two notices, which were posted at the front of the court so that all litigants would be aware.

Zhao Tieqiao's Assassin Arrested 127

丨The main culprit, Zhou Zhizhang, was arrested in the Xian Shi Amusement Park丨

Zhao Tieqiao, the former General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was riding in a car on the morning of April 29, 1920, at 9:00 AM, from his residence to the company to handle business. When he arrived at the front of the company, several thugs suddenly rushed out from the side and fired several shots at Zhao, all hitting vital points. He was rushed to the hospital, but due to the fatal nature of the injuries, he could not be saved and died. The assassins escaped from the scene. Although the authorities offered a reward for their arrest, the thugs fled to distant places and remained at large, making it impossible to capture them. Until the other day, Hua Zong Tan Chang You Agen of the Old Gate Patrol discovered that the main culprit in the case, Zhou Zhizhang (also known as Xuan Si) from Anhui, was playing in the amusement park of the Xian Shi Company. He immediately cooperated with Detectives Liu Junqing, Zhou Guisen, and Detective Li Shugui, and secretly went to the park. They arrested Zhou and his accomplices Xun Gewenqing, Gong Wenjiang, and two women, Jin Zhang and Zhou Xu, and took them to the patrol room. After investigating, it was found that the two women, Jin Zhang and Zhou Xu, were not related to the case and were released. Yesterday morning, Zhou and the others were escorted to the First Special District District Court Criminal Court No. 1, where Judge Qian Hongye questioned them. Attorney Qian Xunjiu of the Patrol Room stated that it had been found that the defendant Zhou Zhizhang was indeed the main culprit in the Zhao Tieqiao assassination case. The two defendants, Ge and Gong, had also committed many theft cases. The Patrol Room is currently investigating the case and should be allowed to detain them. After questioning each of the defendants, Judge Qian ordered them to be returned to custody and rescheduled the hearing for further investigation.

Our bank handles thousands of dollars every day. Would it be good for you to rob our bank? At that time, I was just joking. I did not expect that Hongsheng would later want to rob my bank's money, which I prevented. Hongsheng then told Zhou Heshang about this matter. Two months later, Zhou Heshang called Hongsheng to ask me to discuss it at his house. He committed the robbery and gave me $115. I was really fooled and ask for leniency.

The other five people, Chen Yongde, Liu Jiasheng, Zhou Wu氏, Zhao Shunfa, and Shen Jinrong, are only suspected and there is no concrete evidence. Their confessions are omitted. After verifying the confessions, the squad dispatched officers yesterday morning to cooperate with detectives from the Public Concession Police, and rushed to the box of Zhou Mumu, a maid at No. 544, Xinyu Lane, Meibai 格 Road, to recover the original stolen $100. The team took them for record. It is reported that the squad has detained all the suspects and will continue to investigate the remaining accomplices and handle the case together.

Loaded Dice Guarantee Gamblers Lose Every Time 131

Jin Shude Compensates Due to Guilt

Reports Theft Afterward

Jin Shude, nicknamed Xiaofang, a native of Ningbo, is an unemployed vagrant. Recently, he secretly opened a gambling den at No. 17, Xinjia Garden, Xinzha Road, taking a cut of the profits. Dong Xinhai, a native of this county, was one of the gamblers in the den. From the 12th to the 15th of last month, Dong lost hundreds of dollars every day. Dong later found out that the dice in the gambling den were loaded, allowing the house to control the outcome at will, so gamblers could not win. He was very unhappy and negotiated with Jin without success. On the morning of the 16th, Dong led many people with pistols to Jin's place to demand a return of $500. After repeated negotiations, Jin returned $250 to Dong to settle the matter. Afterward, Jin suddenly went to the police station and falsely reported being robbed, claiming that one of the robbers was recognized as Dong Xinhai. The police, unaware of the deception, recently had Hua Detective Liu Junqing and Zhou Guisen from the Old Zha Police Station arrest Dong on Yunnan Road and send him to the First Special District Court for questioning and detention. Yesterday morning, Qian Hong, the head of the criminal court of the First Special Court, continued the trial in the first criminal court. Dong Xinhai confessed the whole story. The court immediately summoned the doorman of Xinjia Garden, No. 1108, to the court. According to the arrest warrant, "On the morning of the 16th of last month, I heard a lot of noise inside No. 17, which sounded like a dispute. I knocked on the door to inquire. Jin Shude said that he was hosting a banquet and there was nothing else. So I withdrew. Later, I heard the sound of dice being thrown again and went to inquire again. Jin replied that he was taking a concubine to play with, so I withdrew again. Not long after, I suddenly heard someone knocking on the alley door. I went to open the door and saw Dong Xinhai and four or five people enter. Dong and the others were all armed with pistols. Two of them held guns to watch me and dragged me upstairs into No. 17. I immediately heard Dong say, 'Call Xiaobaozi out to talk.' At that time, Jin Shude immediately stepped forward and said that they were all family members and that everyone should talk things out. Dong demanded $500, and Jin gave him $250 before they left. At that time, I immediately wanted to report to the police station, but Jin asked me to wait a moment and he would go to the French Concession one afternoon and then go. So I waited for Jin and then went out. Jin returned home and reported to the police station with me. After Dong was arrested, Jin and his wife, as well as two other hooligans, all told me not to recognize Dong Xinhai, but I refused." Judge Qian said that according to the doorman's testimony, Jin Shude was suspected of running a gambling den. Why did the police not prosecute him? The police lawyer, Ru Bao Yi, immediately stated, "When the doorman reported to the police station, the plaintiff did tell him not to recognize him. At that time, the police station planned to sue Jin, but Jin himself recognized Dong Xinhai, so he was not prosecuted. Now that the court believes that he should be prosecuted, please detain Jin Shude and let the police station investigate and prosecute him." Judge Qian then ordered Jin Shude to be detained and rescheduled the trial for July 8.

However, the funds raised by our society are only tens of thousands of yuan, which is far from enough. Please remit all the donation funds from your association to our society for joint distribution. The merits are immeasurable. Xiong Xiling, President of the Chinese General Association of the World Red Swastika Society, bows respectfully."

Qinghai Expedition to Depart Tomorrow 144

| Taking the Shaanxi-Gansu route to Qinghai; returning via Ningxia and Baotou to Beiping |

The China Borderland Culture Promotion Association, which first organized the Qinghai Expedition last month, has completed preparations. The details are as follows:

(Route into Qinghai) After careful investigation, the expedition's route to Qinghai will be by train from Shanghai to Nanjing, then via the Jinpu Railway to Xuzhou. From there, it will turn west via the Haizhou route to Tongguan. After entering the pass, it will take a bus to Xi'an in Shaanxi, then via Xianyang, Binzhou, and Pingliang to Lanzhou. From Lanzhou, it will travel west to Xining in Qinghai, or other locations. If time permits on the return journey, it will travel northeast from Lanzhou via Ningxia and the Hetao region to Baotou, then via the PingSui Railway to Zhangjiakou, turning south to Beiping, and returning to Shanghai by train.

(Departure Tomorrow) The five members of the expedition are scheduled to depart from Shanghai tomorrow afternoon, expecting to return to Shanghai in early September, with a duration of approximately two months.

(Scope of Investigation) The purpose of this expedition to Qinghai is simply to find suitable locations in the province to prepare for the establishment of several public schools for the Han, Hui, Mongolian, and Tibetan peoples. Therefore, the scope is very simple. However, the Yibu Zhongshan Cultural Education Center has entrusted the expedition to investigate education, agriculture, rural areas, land, economy, nomadic life, industry, customs, religion, and so on.

(List of Members) The members of the Qinghai Expedition have been determined by the association at its fourth executive committee meeting: executive committee members Gu Zhizhong and Lu Yi (both reporters for the Xinwen Bao newspaper), executive committee member Gu Yongzhong, alternate supervisory committee member Shu Yongkang (from the education sector), and member Huang Bokui (General Secretary of the China Mining Society). However, Gu Yongzhong is unable to leave Shanghai due to other commitments. At the same time, Wang Yang, a professor at Tongde Medical College, requested to join the association. This was approved at the meeting, and he will travel to the destination for investigation.

(Funding) At 5:00 PM yesterday, the association held its fifth executive committee meeting. Committee members Yu Tianxi, Zhang Xianmei, Gu Zhizhong, Lu Yi, and Gu Yongzhong were present. First, Gu Zhizhong reported on the funding for the Qinghai Expedition: Zhongshan Cultural Education Center provided 1,000 yuan, Xinwen Bao newspaper provided 400 yuan, Hua An Company provided 200 yuan, Mr. Wu Zhiping provided 200 yuan, and Mr. Zeng Zhongming provided 100 yuan, totaling 1,900 yuan, still short by approximately 400-500 yuan. Next, the expedition route and departure date were decided.

(Broadcast Today) Finally, Lu Yi proposed that frontier work urgently requires greater attention from the Chinese people. It was resolved that before the expedition departs, a broadcast will be made to all sectors of society. It was decided that Ms. Ouyang Kaili, a member of the association, will broadcast from the Ma Lishi New Village San Rui Tang Liji Broadcasting Station today from 4:30 PM to 5:00 PM.

Special Feature: Discussion on the Modernization of China 158

The "Shen Bao Monthly" will publish a special anniversary oversized issue on July 15th, adding a special feature on "The Modernization of China," while the original columns will also be published as usual. The advance notice of its main contents has already been disclosed in the advertising column of this newspaper. Now, the reasons for the publication's discussion of China's production modernization problems are recorded below to promote the attention of the Chinese people to production issues.

What are the gains and losses of fighting airplanes and tanks with broadswords? What is the speed of rickshaws and sailing boats competing with automobiles and steamships? What is the difference in production volume between spinning and weaving with hand-cranked spinning wheels and new-style textile machines, and between plowing with old-fashioned rakes and new-style tractors? Although these are questions that even three-foot-tall children can answer without thinking, we must pay attention to the fact that airplanes, steamships, textile machines, tractors, and so on are all tools created in the industrial revolution over the past one or two hundred years. At the same time, their influence has also changed the old economic, social, and political organizations. Now, the production tools and methods of industrially advanced countries have long been "modernized," and their social organizations are also very different from the situation in the era of pure agriculture and handicrafts. Although their current social organizations have many shortcomings, their "modernization" of production is a great achievement of progress that no one can deny. The situation in industrially advanced countries is like this. Looking back at the current situation in our China, what is it like?

In our China, the standard of living has fallen to the point where most people are lingering in a state of semi-starvation; the strength of external defense is so weak that four provinces have been lost, and there is no way to deal with it! The root cause of this is not that other countries have already "modernized," while many places in China are still stuck in the old ways and have failed to adapt to the modern environment? Therefore, recently, almost every Chinese person has felt the necessity of China's "modernization," and "China's modernization" has become a general call.

Indeed, China's only way out economically in the future is "modernization," but when it comes to China's modernization, there are important issues that need to be discussed. The questions are:

(1) What are the difficulties and obstacles to China's "modernization"? What are the prerequisites for promoting China's "modernization"?

(2) Should China's "modernization" adopt individualism or socialism? "Modernization" promoted by foreign capital or "modernization" initiated by national capital? And what are the steps to realize this method?

We believe that the future of China depends on the answers to these two questions, so we specially solicit the opinions of some experts in the country for an open discussion.

In today's time of national crisis, discussing these two issues may seem too "leisurely." In fact, "How to save China from danger and extinction?" and "Where is China going?" are long-standing questions in everyone's mind. We want to raise these questions and solicit different opinions from various parties. The purpose is to contribute various materials related to answering these questions to the Chinese people. It is not to be high-minded or to escape reality. Now, in order to make everyone understand the meaning of raising these questions, it may be useful to simply state a few more sentences. China's rural areas are currently showing signs of collapse, while industry and commerce are declining, and the import surplus statistics reached a record of more than 550 million taels last year. The danger of the entire national economy going bankrupt is imminent. Why is it still impossible to save it for a while? In other words, what is the root cause of why China's industry has not yet been "modernized"? Because this is an urgent problem that China needs to solve, we want to raise the first question and solicit the opinions of various parties. Secondly, in the past two centuries, various countries have successively experienced industrial revolutions and gone through the process of "modernization," resulting in modern capitalist social organizations. This kind of organization is currently showing many flaws due to the unprecedented global economic panic, and it is shaking. Should China's future "modernization" simply follow their old path, or should it seek a new path? "It is easy to start, but difficult to finish." Since we have raised the first question, the second question must naturally be raised for discussion at the same time.

Since the publication of this journal, it has been one year. We are very grateful for the welcome and love of our readers, which has enabled us to develop day by day. Now we have decided to compile the opinions of various parties on the above two questions in the July issue of this journal and present them to our readers to fulfill our obligations and commemorate the first anniversary of the publication.

Important Education News

Ministry of Education Revises and Announces Regulations for Studying Abroad 159

Each year from April 1st to April 15th, the provinces and cities hold examinations. On the 30th, the Ministry of Education announced the revised Articles 6, 8, 9, and 35 of the Regulations for Studying Abroad. The revised text is as follows:

Article 6: Publicly funded students from various provinces and cities must be re-examined by the Ministry to make a decision. The examination mentioned above shall be held once a year within the same province or city. The registration time is from February 1st to March 1st, the examination dates for each province and city are from April 1st to April 15th, and the re-examination dates for the Ministry are from July 1st to July 15th. However, provinces and cities that are far from Beijing or have other special circumstances may submit a request to the competent education administrative agency for approval to conduct the re-examination at the location of the preliminary examination by personnel dispatched by the Ministry or designated agencies.

Article 8: Anyone who has one of the following qualifications may register for the examination: (1) Graduates of public or registered private colleges or universities at home and abroad, and have held technical positions related to the subject they have studied for more than two years; (2) Graduates of public or registered private colleges or universities at home and abroad who have continued to study the subject they have studied for more than two years and have valuable specialized works or other achievements; (3) Graduates of public or registered private universities or independent colleges at home and abroad who have excellent grades.

Article 9: When registering, in addition to submitting a graduation certificate and two recent 4.5-inch half-length photos (one to be kept by each province or city and one to be sent to the Ministry), those who have the qualifications in the first clause of the preceding article must also submit two copies each of their resume and service certificate (one to be kept by each province or city and one to be sent to the Ministry). Those who have the qualifications in the second clause of the preceding article must also submit specialized works or other achievements. Those who have the qualifications in the third clause of the preceding article must submit a school transcript. The service certificate or school transcript must be signed and sealed by the highest competent person at the service place or the principal of the school.

Article 35: Self-funded students applying for a study abroad certificate must submit a graduation certificate, a guarantee, two recent 4.5-inch half-length photos, a certificate fee of two yuan, and a stamp duty of one yuan. Those who have the qualifications in the second clause of Article 26 must also submit a resume and a service certificate (the service certificate must be signed and sealed by the highest competent person).

A Record of the First Day of the Zhejiang Provincial Middle School First District Joint Examination 161

214 Senior High Students Actually Present

More Than 1,000 Junior High Students Actually Present

(Hangzhou Correspondence) The Zhejiang Provincial Middle School Graduation Joint Examination was held simultaneously in six districts yesterday (the 1st). The situation in the first district is recorded below. The first examination hall was in the auditorium of the Provincial First Middle School. The examinees were senior high school students. From 7:00 AM to 9:00 AM, the examination was on Party Principles, with 214 students actually present. From 9:30 AM to 11:30 AM, the examination was on Physics, with the same number of students present as before. From 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM, the examination was on Chinese, with the same number of students present as in the morning. The second examination hall was in the Provincial Senior High School. The examinees were junior high school students. Because there were more people, they were divided into three places: Hall A was downstairs in the auditorium, Hall B was upstairs in the auditorium, and Hall C was in the rain-covered playground. From 7:00 AM to 8:00 AM, the examination was on Party Principles, with 1,077 students actually present. From 8:30 AM to 11:30 AM, the examination was on Nature, with 1,078 students actually present. From 2:00 PM to 4:30 PM, the examination was on Chinese, with 1,077 students actually present. Half an hour before each subject's examination, the proctors entered the hall to distribute the examination papers and questions. When the students entered the hall, the proctors checked the joint examination certificates, checked the seat numbers, verified the photos, and explained the precautions. The students were able to abide by the examination hall rules, and the order was very good. There were no violations of the examination hall rules. Director Chen of the Hall, Deputy Directors He Jinghuang and Lu Dianyang, and office staff all arrived early to preside over all affairs. The instructors from each school accompanied the examinees and went to each examination hall to wait for the examination. During the examination, the instructors waited in the rest room. According to the examination hall rules, they did not watch outside the examination hall. For the sake of the health of the examinees, the office set up a temporary clinic and hired doctors from the Provincial Hospital, the Municipal Hospital, the Provincial Medical School Clinic, and the school doctors from the Provincial Senior High School, Girls' High School, First Middle School, and Municipal Middle School. Occasionally, one or two students were diagnosed by the doctor on duty as needing treatment and were not suitable to participate in the joint examination. After issuing a certificate, they were immediately advised to seek medical treatment quickly. After they recovered, they would take a make-up exam. Electric fans and ice trays were installed in the hall to circulate the air and reduce the temperature. The examination will continue tomorrow and the day after. It is also reported that the second meeting of the Joint Examination Committee will be held at 4:00 PM this afternoon to discuss the evaluation of the examination papers and the calculation of the results. Committee members such as Wu Dezhang and assisting committee members such as Chen Guobao have arrived in Hangzhou one after another.

After the review, more than 190 of the 500+ students will remain for the next session's make-up exam.

(Jinan Quick News) The Shandong Provincial Second Middle School Graduation Joint Examination was decided by the Education Department Examination Committee to be held in districts on June 1st. After the announcement, there were 581 students throughout the province who failed in two or one subject or were unable to participate in the joint examination due to various reasons. Later, the committee, fearing the suppression of talent, decided to hold a review examination in five districts on June 20th. The examination has been completed, and all the examination papers of the review students in each district have now been reviewed by the examination committee. As a result, more than 340 people passed, and more than 190 people failed. They will be ordered to make up the lessons and take the make-up exam in the next session. Results of the Municipal Elementary School Joint Examination 165

To Be Announced by the Municipal Education Bureau Tomorrow

Make-Up Exam to Be Held on the 6th and 7th

Only eight people have failed in three subjects and should repeat the grade. However, more than 1,000 people have failed in one or two subjects or have not completed the subjects and should take a make-up exam. More than 100 people have not taken the subjects and should take a supplementary exam. The Education Bureau has decided to hold the elementary school make-up exam on the 6th and 7th of this month. The list of students who have passed the elementary school joint examination and should take a make-up exam or a supplementary exam will be officially announced by the Municipal Education Bureau tomorrow (3rd). Because the number of people and names is too large, the Morning News has been specially commissioned to print a special issue on the 3rd to disclose the complete list and give it away with the newspaper so that students from various schools and parents can see it first and do not have to write to the Education Bureau for it. At the same time, the Municipal Education Bureau will publish a notice in major newspapers explaining this matter. In addition, the results of the middle school joint examination will also be announced in the same way on the 5th or 6th and will be published in a special issue with the Morning News. The dates for the middle school make-up exam are said to be the 10th, 11th, and 12th.

Summer School News 174

Shanghai Provincial Middle School: Shanghai Provincial Middle School is utilizing the summer vacation period to provide youth with supplementary instruction in major subjects to prepare them for further studies. It has been running a summer school for five years, with remarkable achievements. Nearly all summer school students have been admitted to the school and other well-known middle schools for further study. This summer, the school will continue to run its sixth summer school, which has been approved by the Provincial Department of Education. Registration began on June 16th and has been very enthusiastic. This year, the school will make full use of the holiday to reduce the burden on students while maintaining the same tuition fees. The duration of the course has been extended by one week (a total of six weeks). The courses offered are the main subjects for entrance examinations at all levels of high school and junior high school. In addition to classes, there are many activities for students, including moral cultivation, health training, lectures by famous people, and summer entertainment. The school will also continue to publish the Summer School Weekly and Overview. It was reported that the school originally scheduled the registration deadline for July 1st and the start of school for July 3rd. However, due to the late holidays for students from afar, who were unable to arrive at school on time, many have sent letters requesting an extension. Therefore, the registration deadline has been extended to July 4th, and classes will officially begin on the 5th.

The facilities are being perfected as much as possible, so registration has been exceptionally enthusiastic in recent days. Ching Yeh Middle School Improves Engineering Program 175

The Municipal Ching Yeh Middle School in this city, in order to promote vocational education, stopped offering senior high school normal courses and changed to senior high school engineering courses. Due to the current social need for talent in surveying, drafting, pile driving, and construction, it was decided to first establish a surveying and drafting group, which has been operating for two years. It is reported that instruments have been added this academic year, costing nearly ten thousand yuan. Construction of a workshop is now underway for practical training. The school has also submitted a request to the municipal government to instruct the public works and utilities bureaus to give priority to employing graduates of the school, in order to promote and benefit the development of vocational education. It is also reported that the first enrollment will be held on July 15th, with vacancies in each grade.

University Students' Joint Announcement: A Letter to Students Returning Home for Summer Vacation 178

Recognize Responsibilities in a Grave Environment

Urge Leaders to Jointly Overcome National Crisis After Returning Home

Encourage Students with De Fichte's Words

The Shanghai University Students' Joint Association held its twelfth executive committee meeting at the headquarters of the Youth Propaganda Corps yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m. Attendees included representatives from Chiao Tung University, Chinan University, Great China University, Soochow University, and Wen Hua University. Kung Shao-hsiung of Chiao Tung University presided. The meeting resolved to (1) issue a letter to students returning home for summer vacation, (2) have all executive committee members participate in the welcoming ceremony for General Ma Chan-shan, (3) send a telegram to Chairman Ho of the Hunan Provincial Government requesting protection and assistance when the association's summer national salvation propaganda team arrives, and (4) contact the radio station to broadcast national salvation propaganda. The meeting adjourned at 5 p.m. The text of the letter to students traveling home for summer vacation is recorded below. In the blink of an eye, the summer vacation has arrived. Students are about to embark on their journey home. The toil of studying for half a year, however, this year's summer vacation is different from previous years. Do not lightly take a step into your home. Before entering your home, take a look around the environment and, even more importantly, clearly understand the responsibilities you should bear in this grave environment. What is the gravity of the current environment? Rampaging Japanese invaders, leaping bandits, internal worries and external troubles, all pressing down. Resisting tyranny and striving for survival, even with the strength of our entire nation, it is difficult to hope for relief. And the leaders within the country are not conscious of this situation, often destroying their own lines of defense. The severity of the environment and the precariousness of the national situation are unprecedented. We young university students hold the future of the country and are the lifeline of the nation. How can we revitalize our country? How can we revive our nation? How can we escape annihilation and achieve survival? The key lies in the hands of us university students. Having recognized the gravity of the current environment, which stems from internal and external troubles, the failure of the country's leaders to unite sincerely and endure for the sake of the country is the greatest reason for the critical national situation. During this trip home, students should lead the people in their localities, urging the country's leaders to go to the capital immediately to jointly overcome the national crisis. The country today cannot defend itself without unity, and it cannot be saved without unification. In addition to this, the students' responsibility during the summer vacation is to continue sharpening their knowledge. Sporadic efforts yield no results. National salvation lies in effective struggle. Studying can cultivate strength and build the foundation for struggle. Acquiring true knowledge will allow you to contribute to society and the country in the future and bear the great responsibility of revitalizing the country and reviving the nation. The famous German philosopher Fichte said in a speech to the German people, "Today, what I expect from those who listen to this lecture is not to be content with the status quo, not to lament the failures of the past and be unable to overcome their grief, not to seek solace after the pain, not to fall into self-abandonment because there is no comfort, not to drift along and get by. What I want from you is that you can extricate yourselves from suffering and engage in clear thought and contemplation. What I want to take you out of the abyss of suffering is not to tell you that external assistance will come, and that there will be changes over time. What I want to tell you is to understand our position, to understand the strength we have left, and to understand the methods for saving ourselves." I dare to offer Fichte's words to my fellow students who are about to leave for their summer vacation as a mirror.
